--- 帖子 #1 ---
Hi guys,

Just wanted to share my idea hoping for good feedbacks from all of you guys. So here’s my idea,

I’m busy doing my job since I’m an employee, so I wanted to have a minimum control of my chart, I just want a daily control, secondly there is no EA that works forever since the market is changing overtime so I have to “drive” the EA manually ( set the EA “Long only” or “Short only”). So far it ganerates at least 500pips per month. It's very simple and easy, I’ll show you how.

1. Put the EA on 5 Min chart
2. Put the template and indicator on your daily chart

How to start and “drive” the EA
1. See the major trend on daily chart just like the pic below,
2. When you see the trend down on daily chart, “Drive” the EA “Short only” on your 5 min chart, and vice versa
3. When you see the trend is changing on daily chart then you have to “drive” your EA on 5 min chart accordingly

The goal for this setting is less stress because you don’t trade news and not sit in front of your computer for a long time, just check it once or twice a day.

How to drive the EA Long or Short only, please refer to word file I attached.

For example:

Try to backtest GBPUSD for 1 month period from 1 August 2008 to 31 August 2008, becouse on that month the market shows downtrend from start to end, set the TP to 100pips, drive it short only and u will get approximately +3094pips in a month. FYI..price range for that month is only 1067pips.

Backtest for EURUSD on Aug 2008, for short only, TP 100pips, u will get approximately +2135pips in a month, and price range is only 1029pips.

Then u get a total of 5229pips in a month of Aug 2008 for those two pair.

This system works great depends on your skills to drive this EA.

Please see the discusion link below for better understanding about this setting.
Start from post 2090 page 140 to post 2168 page 145

http://www.forexfactory.com/showthread.php?t=7200&page=140

For u guys if u need a "TRADE SIMULATOR" u can check this link below.
http://www.forexfactory.com/showpost...&postcount=505

Please demo it for at least 2 month before u trade it live to make sure u get all the things right.
0.01 lot size for every $1000, or
0.1 lot size for every $10,000 is a must...!!!!!

I'll try to sumarize this thread continually updated in a word document to make it easy to read.

English is not my default language.

--- 帖子 #2 ---
Technical question

How do I adjust the EA for 4 digit or 5 digit broker platform?

Try this setting:

5 digit broker platform

SL : 3000 (means 300 pips)

TP : 500 (means 50 pips)

Pipstep : 400 (means 40 pips)

4 digit broker platform

SL : 300 (means 300 pips)

TP : 50 (means 50 pips)

Pipstep : 40 (means 40 pips)

============================================================================

Why does the EA open many position?

pipstep setting

usually 20 open position at the same time is not normal, maybe u should check the setting for the pipstep.

lets me show u this,the default setting for pipstep is 40 pips, then when u open buy position and then the market goes against u for -40pips, then the ea will open another buy position, it will do the same thing when it touch -80pips and so on. so check your pipstep and adjust it to your broker platform, the default is for 5 digit broker platform.

so according to SL for 300 and pipstep is 40 then maximum open position at a time is 300 devide by 40 is 7 maximum open position at a time.

============================================================================

Why does my EA is not working?

Perform this check

1. Have u set the EA to "Allow live trading"?

2. Activate the button "Expert Advisor" on the toolbar

3. Make sure there is a "smile icon" next to your EA on the right top of the chart

4. Adjust the setting according to your broker platform

5. Check the internet connection, since this EA needs a very good up time internet connection.

============================================================================

Can I change the setting for SL, TP and Pipstep? SL is too big for me

Of course yes, as u feel comfort, the point is that I informed u about the major idea of "driving the EA". Just try your optimum setting fits your strategy.

============================================================================

How do I backtesting this EA?

U have to drive the EA according to the major trend even its on backtest, just exactly when U foward test it. drive the EA each time u find a trend reversal in a spesific day.

Like I mention before, try to backtest it for 1 month on Aug 2008, becouse that month the market shows down move from start to end, drive the EA short only and u will see that.

####################################################################

Non Technical question

What did U do when the major trend reverse?

It depends to the market,I usually look for the daily candle pattern as my other indicator, but when the market is about to change I close all the opening position of course. This is what I do when I noticed and assumed that the market is about to change:

1. Safe way, not trade when the market is in the midle of changing direction, and continue to ride the market when the trend is clear, this avoiding drawdown, just take 7 days trading in a month and you probably got 1000pips. Strongly recomended to use this way.

2. Unload the EA and put SL and TP lower (20 - 40 pips) on the opening position, or close all of the opening position even if its negative, and start to load the EA again according to the major trend when I see the major trend is clear.

3.Still trading when the market is about to change, I use this just to confirm when the market is about to changing, when I see the frofit for the day less than 100 pips or even negative (but often still profit but minimum) that means I have to Drive the EA accordingly. But I dont recomend this, I only use this way on the demo.

============================================================================

How do u recognize a clear major trend?

Clear down trend

when the chart turns red and the arrow pointing down and the candle pattern confirm it ( I suggest U to learn candle pattern, I got this suggestion from Phillip Nell with his great 4H MACD strategy), thats where the high probability of the next daily candle move down. if one of this indis is not in the line it means that u have to becareful, or much better not to trade, trade 7 days a month is enough to have "maybe" arround 1000pips.

U can use your own indis as u feel comfort.

Clear up trend

vice versa

============================================================================

Why do you use 300pips for the stoploss?

300 pips is to give space for the market retracment.

from what I know that it is still save as long as u still follow the daily trend, when it's negative dont worry becouse the market will recover it (as long as u follow the daily trend), its normal to have negative open position becouse this EA will open the position on retracment. Let me show u

Lets say the daily trend pointing to move down , but the price dont moves smoothly down right"?,it retrace (against the daily trend for temporary), when it retrace the EA will open position, it means that it will be negative for a while but soon the market will recover your position to positive becouse you follow the major trend.

So make sure that u follow a clear trend.

=========================================================

If you see the trend is clear so why you have to use this EA?

My experience is that this EA can catch pips more than the market pip range , for example from January 1st Jan to January 7th the price move down for 500 pips, then this EA can catch more than 500 pips from the price retracement, just try this EA on back test for 1 month on Aug 2008 you will see that.

=========================================================

What pair do you trade?

I used GBPUSD and EURUSD or you can try another pair, just look for the pair that shows a clear trend in daily chart.

=========================================================

Regards,

Samurai Power

--- 帖子 #55 ---
I have been thinking about this for a while, but not sure I like what I am understanding....

Let's say that you trade with the trend. Okay, a good idae, but that day the pair goes against you. Let's say that it is GbpUsd and moved 400 pips against your trend trade.

Now, every 40 pips that the trade moves against you, it opens another trade with the trend. So, at the end of the day you could literally be down over 2000 pips with 3 trades stoping out at 300 Pips in loss.

Now, the next day the pair trades back with the trend, except it doesn't move against you at all and you take profit at 100 pips. That means that 1 day you lost over 2000 and the next won 100. This is a really scary thought for me.

I will put it on a demo account, because I am not sure if I am understanding the technicals right. I wil determine trend and set the EA accordingly.

<<>>

Instructions from original post:

This "indicator" is actually an EA. The EA does not generate trades, it simply reads the closed orders from your account history.

This version allows you to enter 10 separate currency pairs to monitor. The EA will display for each selected pair the number of closed trades, profit, number of wins, win profit, number of losses, and loss profit for each separate pair. It also will display the totals for all the closed trades, closed profit, closed wins, closed win profit, closed losses, and closed loss profit.

Save this file and attach as an EA. Attach to any chart. Set the chart to a line chart, and select the color for line graph as "None".

--- 帖子 #151 ---
I know why.

Let me show U some example with FOREXflash daily autotrend EA.

First of course u set Long and Short on the EA since this is an autotrend EA right? and u set 200 EMA as a cut off for the EA to reverse the direction.

Like FOREXflash said, the EA won't open SELL if the price ABOVE the EMA, and the EA won't open BUY if the price BELOW the EMA.

Now look at the daily chart pic below with 5 month history.

The the price is BELOW the EMA for the last 5 month, it means it wont buy if the price always BELOW the EMA even if there is an up trend in the daily candle.

See the numbers I pointed in the pic

Number 1 : up move for 1247 pips

Number 2 : up move for 1029 pips

Number 3 : up move for 1028 pips

if U dont do anything of course u are gonna blow your account. Adjust the EMA value on the EA to maximize how the EA to recognize the trend then the EA will open the buy position.

The rules is the same on the 5M Autotrend EA

Regards,

Samurai Power

--- 帖子 #161 ---
Quite new to forex as well as MT4 and want to thank all people on this and other threads for the enthusiasm and ideas.

I have gone through the code posted by ForexFlash and do think there is an issue with brackets. ForexFlash, below i post an extract of a local copy that i made which does seem to do both buy and sell:

if(

MarketAnalize()==-1

&& myMA*(1+Percent/100)<Bid

&& Direction!=22

&& (Bid>=(LastPrice+(CurrentPipStep*Point)) || MyOrdersTotal()==0)

&& RVI<0

) // modified by Renato

{

LogWrite("SELL: " + MarketAnalize() + " myMA: " + myMA + "Bid: " + Bid + "Direction: " + Direction + "LastPrice: " + LastPrice + "MyOrdersTotal: "+ MyOrdersTotal() + "RVI: " + RVI);

OrderSend(Symbol(),OP_SELL,Lots,Bid,slip,Bid+(Stoploss*Point),Bid-(TakeProfit*Point),GetCommentForOrder(),MagicNumber,0,clOpenSell); // modified by Renato

ret = 1;

}

if(

MarketAnalize()==1

&& myMA*(1-Percent/100)>Ask

&& Direction!=11

&& (Ask<=(LastPrice-(CurrentPipStep*Point)) || MyOrdersTotal()==0)

&& RVI>0

) // Go LONG -> Only buy if >= 30 pips below previous position entry // modified by Renato

{

LogWrite("BUY: " + MarketAnalize() + " myMA: " + myMA + "Bid: " + Bid + "Direction: " + Direction + "LastPrice: " + LastPrice + "MyOrdersTotal: "+ MyOrdersTotal() + "RVI: " + RVI);

OrderSend(Symbol(),OP_BUY,Lots,Ask,slip,Ask-(Stoploss*Point),Ask+(TakeProfit*Point),GetCommentForOrder(),MagicNumber,0,clOpenBuy); // modified by Renato

ret = 2;

}

Please check and see if this was the intention.

Fredella

--- 帖子 #208 ---
There is no problem with the ea execution......

EA consist of 2 trading parts, first is to take a trade in the direction of the

daily trend, and the second is to take a few trades acordingly to the ea rules, and that means that you can have one buy, and few sells one after

another no matter what the daily trend is........

regarding the timeframes, use ea on 5min TF, cos ea is intended for that!

--- 帖子 #210 ---
Firstly: thanks to ForexFlash for your work here and others you know who you are.

Secondly: As for all systems we need to have some sort of enter and exit. Its not wise just start EA in the middle of downtrend, retrace can happen any day, and can go over 300pips up.

I put simply CCI (14) on daily chart with zero line, -100 and +100 lines. Now,

for entry (start) could be also used cci crossing zero line with high angle.

For safe exit: or to give EA a day off (pause), we could use cci hitting -100 line from opposite direction than trend (if downtrend). See Picture...

And maybe turn EA on again, when cci breaks -100 line and goes down again.

In backtesting, this looks like safe exit enough. Will do forward test to see how it goes.

Ran FE version all day today on a 5 decimal broker and it never opened a trade. I don't know why.

The EMA(m5)v2 version continues to perform the same as usual, opening longs and shorts with no regard to the 200 ma. It has the same undesirable problems as these "grid" type EAs, in that they will leave lots of unrealized drawdown while they make realized profit. Then some day you have to close all the open positions and there goes your profit.

I'm through testing it. I've seen enough. I wish you the best of luck with it.

--- 帖子 #222 ---
The thing is to be correct on the trend. If you're not, you can not only have big drawdowns, but big losses. Ask 10 people how you can know the current trend will stay that way, and you get 10 different answers. You can go with the last day, the last few days, the last week, or use a moving average cross, or whatever, but I've yet to see anyone get it right consistently. It's fine when the GBP is trending your way and you make lots of pips. Not so fine when it keeps changing, or suddenly reverses, and you're down 200 plus PIPS on 3 to 5 positions.

18679360    2009.02.02 09:17    buy    0.10    gbpusd    1.43197    1.40197    1.44197    2009.02.02 17:05    1.41423    0.00    0.00    0.00    -177.40

18691867    2009.02.02 10:30    buy    0.10    gbpusd    1.42761    1.39761    1.43761    2009.02.02 17:06    1.41459    0.00    0.00    0.00    -130.20

18693263    2009.02.02 10:38    buy    0.10    gbpusd    1.42360    1.39360    1.43360    2009.02.02 17:06    1.41465    0.00    0.00    0.00    -89.50

Here are my 2 questions:

1. Is it supposed to have 7 trades because the ST=300, PipStep=40 from 1.44435 drop to 1.41435? Why do you only have 6 trades?

2. When you got the 3rd trade SL, did you close the rest 3 trade manually or by EA itself? or at that moment you realized you jumped in the wrong trend?

When one jumps in the trend wrong from the beginning,

If he gets the #1 SL, he realizes he was wrong and close all the trades, then he will get 1260 pips of loss for 7 trades.

If he gets the #2 SL, he realizes he was wrong and close all the trades, then he will get 1500 pips of loss for 7 trades.

If he gets the #3 SL, he realizes he was wrong and close all the trades, then he will get 1700 pips of loss for 7 trades.

If he gets the #4 SL, he realizes he was wrong and close all the trades, then he will get 1860 pips of loss for 7 trades.

If he gets the #5 SL, he realizes he was wrong and close all the trades, then he will get 1980 pips of loss for 7 trades.

If he gets the #6 SL, he realizes he was wrong and close all the trades, then he will get 2060 pips of loss for 7 trades.

If he gets the #7 SL, he realizes he was wrong and close all the trades, then he will get 3500 pips of loss for 7 trades.

So before you drive EA, you study the chart, analyze all the indications and MAs, the Loss still will happen. What's the best solution to avoid this, I am thinking of it. Any comments are welcomed.

Great Asamca_jason. I think u pay attention on the detail,..

1. The answer is I don't know why it happened like that asamca, I saw that too when it happened, and i've been wondering why just like u do now. That is happens quite often I guess, when my running position is let say -50pips it didnt opened another position yet, dont know why, maybe its about the code, or maybe the price moves really fast, but i dont know for sure.

2. I knew that if the price goes beyond some level, it might be a trend reversal just like I posted earlier, and when it happen on 2nd Feb i didnt drive the EA on purpose just to show u guys how danger it would be, But the price goes too far beyond my expectation, it closses 3 running position with -300pips each, I think that is enough to show u guys to be aware, then I close the rest opening position manually, then I didnt trade full day on the next day becouse I couldnt read where the trend will go, as u can see on the statement result, then when the trend is clear I jump again just like today.

If I was running it on real acc I will close the running position even its negative before it becomes a nightmare, and jump to the street driving the EA again when the trend is clear.

It is really important not to trade when u feel uncertain about where the daily trend will go.

Yes I study the chart before I decided to run the EA,

1. read news, and another expert analisys

2. historical price action (I didnt have feeling on trading on 2nd Feb becouse when I saw the historical chart the price fell down so hard on monday from several weeks before, but my indis still show me an uptrend, that what makes me aware)

3. draw trend line (important to see support and resistance/psych level)

4. read the candle pattern

5. and of course my indis

6. my mood and my feeling about the trend, when im not in the mood and doubt about the direction i dont trade, even if i have to loose lots of pips.

it seems like a long list but when u experience with it, it wont take too much time.

Regards,

Samurai Power

--- 帖子 #272 ---
Hi,

i have created a version with CCI14, that is, just at the moment the trade is ordered, a check is made if the current daily cci(14) is above a certain threshold (parameterised) in case of a buy order, or below the same but negative threshold in case of a sell order. The cci is calculated with the "typical" price (H+L+C/3). I have also parameterised the averaging period (14) and found that it is best set at 4 instead of 14.

I feel that CCI is also too late to pick trend changes in certain cases, e.g. 19th of Jan 2009 for GBP/USD.

Try it for urself.

Fredella

--- 帖子 #286 ---
Hi, good time to start to learn programming

I will try and integrate some of these ideas, maybe not today but some other time this week. I believe the problem with all these pictures is they provide a view after the event. E.g. the 19th of January was a big down day, however it started of positive. The indicators might well show an uptrend in the beginning of the day, and if you use daily indicators that take the Open value, you might be buying rather than selling. The other issue I found was that when you are backtesting the use of times and days becomes impossible. So for example not trading on fridays or on certain times of the day is not possible in backtest as the DayOfWeek() and TimeOfDay() functions return the current server day and time, not the one during the backtest. I'm thinking if for example only trading during the latter part of the day would be useful, to allow the daily trend to set in properly. However, can not see the effect of that in backtest.

Fredella.

--- 帖子 #287 ---
It's true these indicators look fine after events and in real can give false signals but what is important is to avoid that the EA continues to trade in the wrong direction.

So we need to try different ways to improve the use of the EA.

Hi,

whilst we're going to think about ways to improve, i have here attached a version that seems an improvement to the current CCI one, in that it checks that the CCI is in a trending state, i.e. not retracting back to zero. Try it out and let me know. It will do far less trading then the previous one but it should be more successful. I tried it on G/U and since January 1st it would just hit one SL out of 30 trades. For different currencies you might need to alter the settings.

The other positive note is that backtesting seems very identical to demo trading when i look at the trades the CCI system entered into and when i then compare it to the results of the back test. The only drawback of backtesting remains the issue that you can not do anything with days and times as noted previously.

As always: do not use this EA on a live account.

--- 帖子 #381 ---
Hi Fredella fren,

Well actually I dont know exactly what is, maybe gasgas fren can explain it in detail, but I do know like this, let me give an example about haiken ashi indicator (becouse i think it's happen to many indis):

My daily chart setting on HA is down when u see red, and up when u see white, so when u see a down move the color is red, but sometimes the price moves up and the red color turns white at the spesific day, so when u enter the market when u see red color, and then the price is up and turns white it means u enter in a wrong direction.

Others might have a better explanation.

Regards,

Samurai Power

--- 帖子 #382 ---
I agree this method is not perfect and 3 repaints until reversal trend.

If it was perfect, we would follow up-3,down-3,up-3,....making a lot of money without using EA .

But I noticed when up-3 is fixed and pink star appears, it's generally a downtrend and when down-3 is fixed and yellow star appears, it's generally a uptrend.

As I said it, I'm trading only London session.

Before, I used the pivots-resistance-support with unpredictable results but now I'm using that.

So at London open, I'm checking if 4H trend and 1H trend are in agrement for each pair and then I put "only long" or "only short".

Sometimes, I change the direction during the session if there is a big reversal trend after news for example.

It's important to avoid a dangerous reversal trend and this method is just a tool to protect the EA ....no more.

Just my thought.

--- 帖子 #500 ---
Hi there, thread participants.

Thanks and respect to Samuraj Power and others who work tirelessly to realize the potential of Firebird by Trader Seven

I have been reading through the posts, and backtesting various versions of Firebird, and I have been thinking of ways to filter out losing positions.

Just now it struck me that the price action this EA uses is an oscillation: Lay the seeds on the way up and pick the fruits on the way down, and vice versa. These oscillations occur on different scales, and the biggest scale causes problems for Firebird. It picks long positions occasionally just as the large oscillation is about to turn South and short positions just as a large upward movement is about to commence.

This large size price action wave happens more or less in a range - in other words: it is a range based price movement (not always of course, but often).

Now, a very good indicator to indicate range based turns is the Stochastic. So why don't we apply the stochastic on an appropriate scale as a filter for halting long trades on top of the price action hill top and short trades in the very bottom of the valley?

The default Stoch setting is 5 3 3 - I tried Stoch setting 288 172 172 instead on a five minute chart, and lo and behold, the Stoch 'value' line appeared below 20 just as a short trade would have been disastrously wrong and above 80 when a long position would have lost one money. Isn't it marvellous?

This also means that both long and short trades can be taken at other times when this over sized Stoch is neither oversold or overbought.

The version I checked this out with is [Firebird v63G trader seven]. If one of you super intelligent coders could stick a Stoch filter in there I think we'll be successful and very rich, all of us. (...I hope)

Cheers

Divyendu

For the guys trying to automate this Ea. I wanted to try and contribute something that i personally use in my trading also to determine reversal of daily trend that seems to be very exact for me on trending pairs. It is based on price itself instead of cross overs,and I personally believe it has something to do with the fibonaci mathematical phemona. One of the main numbers in fibs is .5 or 5.. the pros generally like a .5 retracemnt. There seems to be something very profound about that number in the universe.

My obervation doesnt really have to do with fibs but i feel it is tied in somehow. i am pretty new to to forex so im no pro, just making observations.

Instead of a MA crossover or at least in combination with an ea crossover, if you plot a 5 period ema on any chart, doesnt matter the tf. If price CLOSES above the 5 period ema then trend is up. If price CLOSES below the 5 period ema then trend is down and usually continues to do so. It works on any time frame any pair and is great sign to exit a trade or keep an eye on opening a new one. Now it is not 100% perfect as nothing is but on daily charts is much more reliable and could help identify trend reversal if ti could be coded in with the ma crosses and such.

sure hope it may help

bulls

ps real live use would be to look @ eu right now on daily. plot the 5 period ema. you would see that price HAS closeD above 5 period ema and we could be looking @ a temp revesal. we got price action AND close above 5 ema and i like trix,,,is also showing green, bounce off lower end of channel. all good signs, but eur is weak so how much up we'll see.

--- 帖子 #508 ---
Hi xchaparro, Fredella, and others

I did some chart studies (see post 500), and here are some filter settings that would cut down the risk for bad trades quite a lot.  Of course some good trades would be affected, but the overall winning statistics I feel could be improved if something like this could be implemented:

Stoch + ADX  filter: apply on [Firebird v63G trader seven]

Indicators on 4hour time base

Stoch 15, 9, 9

ADX 28

1) ADX falling and Stoch within 30/70 = all trades accepted

2) ADX falling and Stoch over 70 or below 30= no positions entered in the direction of oversold / overbought

3) ADX rising and Stoch within 20/80= no position entered against Stoch direction of travel

4) ADX rising and Stoch beyond 20/80 = no trade

The specific settings of what would constitute overbought/oversold could be made external to allow calibration.

I will try to think of the code myself, but I'm afraid I'm terribly amateurish, most likely to introduce bugs as big as your fist...

D

--- 帖子 #516 ---
Hi Gasgas

My thought is that the filter will filter out bad trades, so there should be no need to manually block long or short positions.

It must be stressed that this is not yet tested and is certain not to work yet in many cases - so no live trading with this one yet!!

The target for developing a fully automated EA should be to put the odds more and more in ones favor - for the filters to kill off more bad trades than good ones (in pip value), and to lessen the likelihood of big drawdowns (larger positions can then be entered without too much risking blowing ones account).

I have one more idea for putting the odds in our favor:

Bad trades need to travel all the way to the stop loss which is further away than the take profit level. Therefore bad trades are normally longer lasting than good ones. Lets say for the sake of argument that most of the good trades in a particular currency cross last no more than 100 bars and most of the bad trades last more than 150 bars. Then it would be possible to put a trade-kill function at 125 bars.

It would kill a long position as soon as the Stoch cycle reaches a peak and a short position as the Stoch cycle reaches a valley.

In this way a loosing trade could be less costly by many many pips.

This type of function is beyond my comfort level to code, so please, anybody with the skills.. We need your help!

D

--- 帖子 #523 ---
Hi Tokken

Glad to see your positive result

Fredella, hope we can find a solution to your bad result

The first idea: to filter out potentially disastrous trades with the help of a combination of ADX and Stoch - it needs calibration as per the commonly occurring price action on each different pair. Is it easier to just make separate copies of the EA for separate pairs, just to avoid complexity?

The larger price fluctuation (the one that out-runs the existing stop loss) has to be mirrored as far as possible by the Stochastic read out. Different values have to be tried out until it looks right. I doubt this calibration can be automatized, it is just a matter of visually making sure that Stoch hits overbought at the same time as the price produces one of those large peaks - and a valley for oversold. the Stoch values can also be external values (in the EA code) allowing for back testing and fine tuning it for each currency pair. This system of filtering trades can prevent any trade at all in a strong sustained trend (Perhaps then another trend following system can be put to good use. The problem is to know when the trend is at an end!!).  I think the ADX value is pretty robust and does not need to be different for different pairs.

The second idea - to kill off trades that fail to hit Take Profit before they have a chance to hit Stop Loss (see post 516) - it would be nice if some more competent programmer could set it up. I'm just a beginner.

Again: That trade killing parameter has to be calibrated to the price action of each pair, and it has to be double blind tested to see if it actually increases profit or decreases risk.

Please note: the EA I posted quotes values suited to brokers using five decimal places.  ;D

--- 帖子 #541 ---
Hi tokken

The EA works in mysterious ways

I am not 100% familiar with the logic that drives the position taking of the EA - without our attempted additions of filters etc. Just because the daily trend is up doesn't mean the EA will take all possible long trades

Thanks for your encouragement to do more work on this project. At the moment I am hammering out a bum-trade filtering system based on a long range Stochastic that would be dynamically re-calibrated by a long moving average, as the topping out levels of Stoch depends a great deal on which way the trend goes.  Please don't have any unrealistic expectations of a fool proof system.  We are just trying to change the odds a little

Take care

One thing I have learned is that:

1) when testing EA's backtesting can be used as sort of a first hurdle or test for your EA to decide whether to keep or toss in the junk pile, but really tells you zip regarding whether or not the EA will be profitable in forward testing.

2) Trading live will be a little different than the results you get on a demo account.

Sure Shogun, it is Firebird V63H04 and can be found here: http://www.accrete.com/fx-mirror/mt4...a-archives.htm

It made 9 winning trades of 18 pips and 1 losing trade of 42 pips for a total of +120 pips. This was on the EurUsd currency alone during about a 14 hour period (From Thurs night 9pm E.S.T to Friday 11 am E.S.T.)

Interesting is that the losing trade was a Sell EurUsd order. If I had been "Driving" the Ea I would have noticed that there was definitely an up-trend on March 12,13 so would have had the EA set to "Long Only". However on the flip side 4 out of the successful 9 trades it made were Sell orders so it would have actually came out worse off overall if I had done that.

What I will probably end up doing is running two simultaneous tests: One with the "Drive" strategy, and one without.  This EA seems to have some extra safeguards built in compared to the V63G, so may be interesting to see which test comes out with more profits.

--- 帖子 #632 ---
Hi sergie and all,

I think u miss a little information about how to backtest this system,

did u drive it correctly? (even its on backtest)

Use a trade simulation application i post in the few pages earlier to find days when the trend continue up or continue down, or when the trend flat based on the daily THV template. MARK THOSE DATES.

And then drive the EA on backtest based on those date u marked, EACH DAY COUNT, treat it exactly just like when u foward test it, the skill on finding the right direction at the particular date on THV daily template is determining the result of the backtest (gives u a big picture of the result on foward test in demo or real account), the more expert your skill on recognizing the daily trend the more better the result.

Let me give u an example how to backtest.

Put the THV daily template on the trade simulator, let say for a period of 1 month (Jan 1st 2009 to Jan 31 2009), then u click start.

When its simulating the market u analyse each day trend, then mark those dates and give a note about trend direction, lets say this is the result:

(simple example)

1. Jan 1st 2009 - Jan 7th 2009 the trend is down.

2. Jan 8th 2009 - Jan 11th 2009 the trend is flat.

3. Jan 12th 2009 - Jan 15th 2008 trend is up.

4. Jan 16th 2009 -Jan 31st 2008 trend is down.

then based on that note, backtest it and drive the EA, and see the result.

Like i mention before, treat backtest exactly just like when u foward test it. Trade when the daily trend is up or down, and dont trade if u find the daily trend is flat.

On foward test u do analyse the daily chart and make a desicion to enter, still continue trade, or stop right? and u get the result.

Its exactly the same...

U analyse daily chart from trading simulator,

and u get the result from backtest.

The general idea is really simple.

Ok, now u can re-backtesting it again, and post the result for 2 years of period for EURUSD pair (if u have time).

Please remeber this.

"KNOWING HOW TO DETERMINE DAILY TREND AND HOW TO DRIVE THE EA IS REALLY..REALLY IMPORTANT."

Regards,

Samurai Power

This will probably sound strange but it was just a gut feeling that something was not right. They seemed more concerned with pushing users to sell more copies with their silly affiliate contests, then they were in making sure the system stays profitable.

With 100,000 people using the same program which initiates trades at the exact same time something's gotta give sooner or later its just common sense. I realize they have updated it so that users have more control now, but I dont think that is going to solve the problem.

Also when it did have a losing trade it was a large loss, usually 2 or 3 days worth of trades, and it would happen fairly often. I guess Im just uncomfortable with a completely automatic EA, just cant be possible unless its updated all the time IMHO.

I prefer the semi-automatic system dealt with in this thread, seems fairly promising but only time will tell.

--- 帖子 #717 ---
Hi there, welcome to the thread. I find the simplist thing to do is just right click whatever file you want to move, click copy then....

Go into your Broker Folder on your computer, it is usually located here:

My Computer / Program Files / Your Broker eg. FXPro/ Experts

once you are in the Experts Folder just right click and paste the EA and restart your Trading Platform, you should now find the EA on the left side bar under Expert Advisors. Either drag it onto your chart or right click and choose "Attach".

If you want to add custome indicators paste them in here:

My Computer / Program Files / Your Broker/ Experts/ Indicators/

If you want to add in a template paste it here:

My Computer / Program Files / Your Broker / Templates

Hope that helped.

Serge

--- 帖子 #728 ---
Usually Fibs are areas to Take profit and close your trade.  The 38% 50% and 61.8 levels are retracement levels to take notice.  The 38% being the most conservative and the 61.8* more optimistic.  Beyond those points could me a change in the direction of the overall trend.

--- 帖子 #743 ---
Hey All, yes I am using a Demo Account, here is basically what I am doing.

I am using the v63H04 version with Max orders = 5

I started using TP=100, SL = 300 about half way through, before that TP=50. Everything else is set to default.

I am trading the EurUsd, GbpUsd, and UsdCad all the same way.

Basically I am looking for the trend on the H4 and D1 charts using the THV indicators provided by Samurai.

I would usually prefer waiting for a nice Heikin-ashi candle (without any shadow pointing in the opposite direction) on the D1 chart, as this is a pretty good indication that the trend is heading that way. I will also take a look at the H4 and see what has been going on for the previous 12 hours or so.

As for the GbpUsd Short today, I have been basically using the H4 as my indicator.

Sometimes if the D1 is showing a reversal with a yellow bar and cross configeration HA candle, I will scroll down to the H4 chart and the trend has been heading solidly in the reverse direction for 8 hours or more I will set the EA to trade accordingly. This one is a bit more risky as the D1 chart has not actually confirmed the reversal yet (yellow bar, and doesn't have decisive HA candle) but can be very profitable if the trend continues.

I will probably get burned with this one sooner or later. For example right now I have a sell on the EurUsd that has a 100 pip downdraw. The reversal that began about 12 hours ago has been wavering.

You will see that I closed a couple of my orders at -60 and -30 pips. I did this when it seemed clear that the trend I was following had come to an end based on the fib resistance level being hit, currency being oversold/overpurchased, and price reversing. Decided to cut my losses.

Namrettik was kind enough to suggest using the Fib Pivot indicator which is also a good way to make an educated guess on how far a trend may go before a reversal.

Hope this helps, and hopefully my results are not just a case of good luck so far, lol.

--- 帖子 #752 ---
Nice sergiel fren. Thats exactly what i'm doing, u know this really well now.

Let me give U guys a simple illustration for easy understanding.

Imagine that the EA is your car, and the indicators is a GPS reciever.

U drive the car based on the GPS signal, weather it turns right, left or straight. But sometimes when u find an intersection on the street the GPS is not giving u a clear signal, that makes u feel doubt on taking the right direction. So U stop your car and wait untill the GPS gives u a clear signal again. That will cost u time a bit to reach your destination, but it will save u from wasting lots of time if u take the wrong direction.

This is exactly the same, knowing when to stop for a while is an important thing also.

Regards,

Samurai Power

--- 帖子 #769 ---
Thanks Sergiel...

With other FB versions, the TS works like this:  If you have TS = 30, and your trades don't go the full TP, it will take you out at +25 pips profit.  If the TS = 40, it will take you out at +35 pips profit.  It worked well for me with a TP = 50 and TS = 40, so if the price didn't make it to 50, at least I would get 35 pips, and not risk reversing and going into a death hang for days.

With the Drive method however, it may be a moot point.

If I had left them going until the time of this post I would have had an additional 150 pips loss and be closing in on the stoploss on one of the trades.

When you get to the end of a trend you will have to make those decisions or be willing to lose your entire stoploss. On three trades I was out for 340 pips loss. If I left the trades going to the stoplosses that would be a total of 900 loss. I would rather take the 340 loss and make it up once the trend was certain again.

--- 帖子 #787 ---
Does this chart mean if we are trading with a $300 stoploss we should only have 4 positions open?

what does this mean. 1 lot per $1000 (is this per mini lot)

Below a list of how many pips drawdown you get:

1 position: 30 pips

2 positions: 90 pips

3 positions: 180 pips

4 positions: 300 pips

5 positions: 450 pips

6 positions: 630 pips

7 positions: 840 pips

8 positions: 1080 pips

9 positions: 1350 pips

10 positions: 1650 pips

And that's excluding the $1000 it takes to buy 1 lot.

So if you want to trade 10 positions you need to set the stoploss at 1650+29=1679 pips.

That's $16790 drawdown plus $10000 for buying the lots. Total $26790 account needed

--- 帖子 #817 ---
Thanks for the clarification. I didn't notice there was such a note (//0=close, 1=HL )in the source. Besides, I am not a programmer and so I don't understand most of the code ...

However, 0=close (of last bar) usually equals to open of current bar. So these two expressions should be understood to mean the same thing. And 1=HL means high and low of last bar. Thus the manual and the note in the program should be interpreted to mean the same thing:

MA_type

- Type 0 calculates its bands using the current bars open.

- Type 1 uses previous bars high for the upper band and previous bars low for the lower band.

- Type 1 trades a little less that Type 0 but it's entries are usually closer to the reversal point.

- So:Type 0: More less certain trades.Type 1: Little less trades that are more certain. With better potential for trailing stops.

Hope I am right... RS

--- 帖子 #818 ---
Thanks for the insight.  I will experiment with both of them.  I have been using the setting = 0 so far with good results.

Congressman Peter DeFazio introduced H.R. 1068:  “Let Wall Street Pay for Wall Street's Bailout Act of 2009” on 13February2009.  This bill imposes a 0.25% transaction tax on the “value of the sale and purchase  of financial instruments such as stock, options, and futures contracts.” While  HR1068 seeks to engender populist appeal by ostensibly exacting monetary  retribution against the big Wall Street firms for wreaking havoc upon the  American financial system, its effects will hurt EVERY American who trades  professionally as well as the ordinary investor trying to save for the future.  The 0.25% tax is invoked against the VALUE of every purchase AND sale of typical  financial instruments, resulting in an egregious added cost borne by every  American for each investment or trading transaction they make, even within the  realm of an IRA or 401K account. It is particularly grievous that this tax is  imposed upon the transaction itself, regardless of whether the purchase / sale  generates a profit. The bill will have virtually no effect upon the behavior of  the relatively few Wall Street executives whose reckless decisions contributed  to the current financial crisis, as added costs would in all likelihood be  passed on in some form to customers. Further, the bill would have the effect of  diminishing capital provision, as it discourages investment to a degree even  beyond the negative impact of capital gains taxation.
HR1068 MUST BE STOPPED!! THE BEST WAY TO ENSURE  HR1068 NEVER BECOMES LAW IS TO MAKE YOUR OPPOSITION FORCEFULLY AND UNAMBIGUOUSLY  KNOWN TO YOUR CONGRESSMEN AND SENATORS!!!
HR1068 is currently in Committee [House Ways and  Means] for markup and debate, so Congress needs to hear from traders and  investors quickly and massively in opposition. Further, the bill has already  garnered air time in the media, thus it is gaining visibility.
Attached/below is a pre-composed letter response  for your use in writing to your Congressmen and Senators. However, be advised  that the most effective means of response in voicing protest regarding HR1068 is  to call your Congressman's/Senators' office. The next most effective means of  communication is via actual mail. The least effective [though still viable]  means of communicating your displeasure regarding HR1068 is via email. You can  obtain the contact information for your Congressman and Senators via http://www.govtrack.us/congress/. You can track the current status of HR1068 as it goes through the legislative  process via  http://www.govtrack.us/congress/bill.xpd?bill=h111-1068 .

Not being a programmer I am a little hesitant in posting this but.....I think that MA Type refers to the type of MA as follows:

0= Simple

1= Exponential

2= Smoothed

3= Weighted

On what the MA is calculated I don't know. Most MA's are calculated on the closing price of the bar but there are other options also. Hope this helps.

--- 帖子 #825 ---
Helo, very good questions. I actually never gave alot of thought to how the increasement would work with the "Driving" method. I just had a gut feeling that it was better to have a somewhat exponential pipstep as opposed to a straighy linear pipstep. I suppose the need for this is reduced when you are "Driving" the EA, however sometimes the price can make big a big retrace quickly and I think this setting will help it find the real bottom/top of a pullback. But I could be completely wrong.

And in regards to max orders, I believe Samurai is correct, it will only set the max orders for that particular pair, not for all currencies running on your platform.  So if you are trading 3 pairs you could still have 15 open orders at once.  I am considering dropping this setting to 4 or maybe even 3.  I think by the time it opens 5 orders in the wrong direction its safe to say there is a trend developing in the wrong direction and not just a pullback.

Cheers

Hi all,

I've been thinking about how to remove judgement (emotion) from the process of pulling the trigger on the EA and when to switch it off again.

On the THV template it would be very straightforward to switch the EA on in Short only mode when the daily bar opens below the Ichimoku cloud and switch the EA off on the first bar that touches it again, opposite applies to a bar opening clear above the cloud.

I have backtested for 2008 & 2009 to date using this rule and the results are attached.

In summary:

2008 - 23580 pips

2009 - 8907pips

The real results, with a few additional rules and understanding of candle price action should be better than the backtest results as no account was taken of weekends; backtest periods ran from the opening of the first candle clear of a cloud to the first candle that fully breached the cloud (see chart) - in reality, price action and proximity to the cloud would give good indication to stop new trades being placed by the EA before the trend reversal hit.

I'm not too familiar with the Ichimoku cloud and don't know if it repaints but watching it today would have been a no trading day on G/U.

I'd appreciate anyone's thoughts on this as the results look promising with manageable drawdowns and the EA would be 'live' for most of the time.

Backtest SL: 300, TP 75, MA type 1, MA TF 5, Max open trades 5

Other settings default

--- 帖子 #838 ---
Is too simple read my indicators:

Xpma it's a simple MA, but you can select MA type and MA period, (on my chart is set to 21, like original template) when trend changes, color of MA changes and has alert.

ADX crosses are the arrows on my chart, only show the crosses of Average Directional Movement Index (Standard metatrader indicator), and shows changes of trend too, (For me its better than MA crosses, less signals but more accurate).

Aroon indicator its a great tool to detect trend changes, This indicatos has two lines (on my chart blue and red), when blue its above red indicates a uptrend, when red above blue downtrend, more separate the lines, more strong is the trend.

You can learn more about Aroon on this link
http://www.investopedia.com/articles...g/06/Aroon.asp

I need a alert on aroon crosses because i'm trading 10 pairs at the same time, and its the key of my system. (i only trade on aroon crosses, if the rest of indicators are in agreement, and always in the direction of the major trend).

Last night i added a silvertrend indicator set to weekly timeframe to detect major trend.

I atach silvertrend indicator and screenshot of my template.

Rules are:

1- Aroon cross.

2- Confirmation with ADX, Heiken hansi and Xpma.

3- Never enter long when Silvertrend (set to weekly timeframe -10080-) are red, and viceversa.

Is a stress less system, I only need be alerted when Aroon changes, then see if the rest of indicators are in agreement.

Hope this help.

--- 帖子 #843 ---
I have been backtesting a way to consistantly enter and exit trades while driving the Firebird EA using the THV3 Trend Indicator to confirm the beginning and end of the trend. There are going to be times that the market will change to yellow(flat) then back again to the trend but if you exit consistantly you should not have as much drawdown.

I marked a few entry and exit points. Green verticle line entry and red verticle line exit.

Rules:

Long Entry - Enter on second green bar if in long position and then exit on next bar after a yellow or red bar forms. Heiken Ashi must be white to enter. (the exit is always at the change of the daily candle)

Short Entry - Enter on second red bar if in short position and then exit on next bar after a yellow or green bar forms. Heiken Ashi must be red to enter. (the exit is always at the change of the daily candle)

Please backtest and give me your input. I am trying to keep this simple and limit drawdowns when the trend changes.

Note the 1/2/09 entry was not on the second bar because of the holiday on 1/1/09.

--- 帖子 #851 ---
All the indicators go into your "inidicators" folder which you can find by looking:

My Computer / Program Files / Your Broker / Experts / Indicators

The template needs to go in the templates folder

My Computer / Program Files / Your Broker / Templates

Restart your platform, open a chart, go to templates, and open the THV template, should be good to go.

The EA is something different, your EA needs to go in the experts folder, then you find it on the left bar under Expert advisors and attach it to your chart.  I find it best to open 2 charts for each currency pair.  One for the EA alone and one for all the template / indicators.

Hope this helps

--- 帖子 #878 ---
I studied many 4 hour charts to look for major reversal points, and I've noticed that a majority of big price reversals take place at the 8 am candle close EST, ie: the NY market opening, which is also after lunch in London/Europe, one of the most active times in the market.

The 2nd biggest turnaround point is the London open, or the 4 am EST candle close.

I also use an RSI 3 to show me the wave strength of the price and when it is over bought or over sold, implying a potential reversal.

Just some food for thought and observation.

--- 帖子 #880 ---
One more thing...

I learned this technique from a manual system I studied.  When a trade is around 50 pips in profit, and all other indications show that it's not likely that it will reverse, I set the SL to the entry price + 1, so if it does reverse, I'll get stopped out and still make 1 pip.

But more important is that it means that this trade is now 100% safe and running on bank money, so you can now turn on the EA on another trending pair to take an additional trade without increasing your risk, ie: you still only have 1 trade at risk.

I've seen many instances where there are multiple simultaneous trends, so this should be a viable concept.

--- 帖子 #937 ---
Hi Guys,

This is gonna be a long one so grab a coffee or fast forward!

Experienced traders will know and understand all of this but hopefully newbies or less experienced folk may find something of use here.

I pointed a senior member friend to this thread and his comment was that the EA looks good but every other post on the thread seems to be someone trying to find the perfect indicator or timeframe to define the trend and therefore eliminate drawdowns - it ain't gonna happen and if you are waiting for that perfect set of indis, you're never gonna pull the trigger and go live!

The THV template gives more trend indis than you can shake a stick at and if you use more than 2 or 3 of them you'll never be able to make a decision - use one or two that suit you, backtest your results and base your strategy on them, switch all the others off or you'll remain confused.

Samurai gave a sound piece of advice at the beginning - look at the news and add this to your analysis - don't let it form your decisions.

The most recent posts now seem to be advocating looking at ever shorter timeframes because this week most currencies are ranging and making it difficult to come to a long or short decision - well - look at the news; we've got the G20 summit in London this week and NFP on Friday. The markets are unsure which way to go but general concensus is that $ strengthens during these summits.

General concensus of Euro is that it is due to weaken in the short term. Another article on the AUD sugests that it is unlikely to strengthen much more before weakening against the USD. This is only what I've read so I don't know if it's good info or bad but it helps me to make a decision, combined with my analysis of the indicators that I've chosen to use.

Let's look at the way the EA works; it places trades on retracements - every 40 pips on my settings. If you micro manage the EA on a 1 or 4 hour timeframe and get jittery every time it retraces you stop it from trading the way Samurai suggests and you will only ever close trades that are in drawdown - if you have even allowed the EA to place them in the first place.

You will get to the bottom of a long trend littered with closed losing trades with virtually no winning trades yet when you back test it later it will show you should have made 1500+ pips!

Going back to the first point - did the backtesting of your strategy show that long term you would be profitable with your strategy? If so, leave the EA alone to do its work - this is emotion at work which doesn't play a part in back testing but certainly does when you pull the trigger on a live account!

So let's look at a trading situation; you're trading 3 $ pairs, SL=300, max orders=5, step=40. You are driving short and the price has spent a day retracing. Have you switched the EA's off or has your analysis given you the confidence to stick with your plan and leave the EA to do its job?

In a worst case scenario you have 15 open orders and are close to your first SL position. This means you are (3 x -280) + (3 x -260) + (3 x -220) + (3 x -180) + (3 x -140) = -$3240 floating based on 0.1 lot / $10000 account. Ok - it wouldn't look like this in reality but you get the picture?

Now, if this is too rich then you will be very tempted to start interfering with your trades. If your strategy is sound and properly backtested then you will leave it alone - you may SL out on one or two but the winners will cover it and long term you will win. Remember - your backtesting assumes you will leave all trades to run and the very positive back testing results that this EA gives are based on long term (daily timeframe) results.

So - to summarise:

Find two max indis that suit you to indicate the daily trend

Keep an eye on the news and don't try to change your strategy to suit every week's chart pattern - understand why the charts are behaving as they are and switch off if necessary.

Have faith in your strategy and backtesting so you can leave your emotions out of the picture when you go live

Make sure that your settings match you money management rules.

This is a large timeframe EA which means big numbers, potentially big profits, potentially big floating drawdowns but fortunately, according to my backtesting, not too many big stop losses and thus emotion will always play a big part.

If the emotions attached to this size timeframe are too much then how about reducing your SL & TP's by a factor of 10 and backtest it on 4 hr or 1 hr trends?

Only trade 1 pair?

Reduce Max open orders or increase Pip step settings?

All of this is just imho - don't mean to lecture but hopefully bring a slightly different perspective to the use of this great EA.

Hi All

Thot this might be relevant since another NFP day is around the corner

It is from a blog I read daily from fxstreet.

Which is important - NFP data or traders positions?

Posted on March 6, 2009 at 15:59 in Market comment,  Market forecast,  Operators' intentions by Dr. S. Sivaraman

When traders avoid taking positions before NFP data release the market made subdued moves before and after the announcements.Then when the players found that the traders with bearish feel shorted yesterday EURO and GBP during drop and are waiting for ‘risk aversion move after NFP data,the players firmed up to hit their stops or induced them to do the short covering.Later when traders developed the bullish feel and bought EURO and GBP on breakout trades,the players are now making the drop to hit their stops on the downside.later they are expected to rise again EURO and GBP for week end.So it is not NFP data which is important for the players to make moves in the market ,actually it is traders pending positions to hit their stops.So the players are more focused on their profits,but traders want to know more about the economy of various countries day in and day out.Who is smart?

--- 帖子 #963 ---
Hi All

I have been testing again and here is a "short" summary. (After another 100pips booked on USDCHF today, there is a lot of incentive to do this ...lol)

I am testing the effect of the TP, DVLimit, Divergence Limit and Percent - settings on Drawdown, Profits and number of trades on the GBPUSD between 17-12-08 and 30-12-08

For this I am using the default setting for most of the parameters (http://www.forexfactory.com/showpost...&postcount=949)

The first test is to see the effect of percent of the drawdown and no. of trades, So I used the range 0.01 to 0.1 (pass 1 to 10 optimisation report_percent see file in the atachement). From this it clear that lower percent setting makes slightly more profit (100pips) but higher drawdown. Now the decison have to be based on the answer to this question will be can you stomach additional 3% drawdown for just 100pips? The answer will definitely be personal.

For the next test (Divergence Limit) I used the 0.1 (6.67% drawdown not different from 0.09 percent setting). Here the Divergence limt range of 0.001 to 0.01 was used. Results shows that pass 6 and 7 - 0.006, 0.007 (Optimisationreport_dvlimt file in attachement) has the right mixture of risk and profit by my judgement (i.e. drawdown and profit).

These conclusions (Percent - 0.1, Divergent Limit - 0.006) was carried forward into the next test to see the effect of the DVLimit (I have no idea if it is different from the Divergent limit above but let see). I used the range 10 to 100 (10 passes). For this test I couldnt find any difference at all for the whole range, drawdown same and profit the same (OptimizationReport_DVLimit10-100.htm). So I am keeping that setting at 10 - the default, until there is more information to support changing it.

Finally, I tried the effect of TP using the range 500 to 3000 (I am using a 5digit broker). Remember for this I am also carrying forward the setting from the three previous test. The results (OptimizationReport_TP500_3k.htm) pass 1- 6 = 500, 1000, 1500, 2000, 2500, 3000. In my opinion TP 1500 and 2000 is just about right for GPBUSD, according to this test as they produce nice profit and lesser drawdown with a lesser number of trade. One could also argue for TP 2500  as well since it produced the highest profit but the let down is that it has the highest drawdown.

Thats it for now, the next stage will be to look into another time window and see how these settings will perform.

Hope I didnt bore you too much.

My regards

Keep on Pippin

Hope every1 took pips on GBP this morning just bagged 146.4pips (150pips TP). I am using the 5-8EMA arrows on the daily in conjunction with candle (HA) colour. News, whatever doesn't really matter I still drive it the way the prices are telling me. For those who are still looking for some of the best trend indicators to use for daily TF, you may try any of the two attachments. The 'Nonlag MA' is good in picking a change in trend while 'Trend' is good in predicting an impending turn. I do use both indicators for 2 daily charts for a currency pair to see if they agree... and have been doing so with good success.

Cheers!

--- 帖子 #990 ---
I've been looking into this as something of a supplemental strategy since I usually only trade the London session manually.

I noticed something with your updated EA that might affect performance:

In the "Firebird-v63H04 (EA) 5 digit platform.mq4", MaxOpenOrders defaults to 5. In the old TS one that you posted before, the default was 10.

If I remember correctly, your method is to use all defaults except for the TP, SL, and PipStep (100-300-40) so the above would actually affect your performance since it won't open any more positions after the first 5 increments of your pipstep.

Maybe I'm misinterpreting the use of that setting (MaxOpenOrders), but I just thought I'd point this out since it may actually impact your testing of this system.

(On the side note, the "5 digit platform" part is appropriate for any IBFX users here -- I just received an e-mail saying they're switching their live accounts to 5 digit quoting as of next week. So if anyone's using Firebird with IBFX, the currently posted version is appropriate.)

Anyway, keep up the good work, everyone.

Hi All

What a day, lots of pips in the bag and lots to report as well

Firstly Gasgas Thanks, I can gladly confirm that the yen fix version is superior to the v63g FB for Yen crosses. So for everyone that's the conclusion from my testing (confirming Gasgas findings).

Ok now to the issue of 5min MATF or 15min MATF. I have attached my results of ten trend I could identify from January till today on GBPUSD. And on these results I carried out a Ttest (dependent variable) and a Sign Test for confirmation (For those well versed in statistics, they will know what I mean -  for other it is all not so complicated). To cut the long story short, there is no statistical difference between the two (a look at the excel file will tell the story)

Below is the setting I used

MA_timeframe=(5 or 15); MA_length=10; MAtype=0; Percent=0.1; TradeOnFriday=1; slip=100; Lots=0.1; TakeProfit=1500; Stoploss=3000; Fast_Period=23; Fast_Price=1; Slow_Period=84; Slow_Price=1; DivergenceLimit=0.006; PipStep=400; IncreasementType=0; DVLimit=10; PipsGoal=5000; PipsLoss=5000; GMT=0; DST=0; OpeningHour=0; ClosingHour=24; writelog=0;

As you can see I am using Divergence Limit 0.006 and TP 1500, carrying forward previous finding for those setting in my earlier post.

NFP, NFP...what can I say, hope you guys can see that it doesnt really matter much what is coming thru the news to drive this EA. Once you can identify the trend correctly, there will have to be a big calamity to turn everything upside down (that doesnt happen often).

So for me, for the day - a friday for that matter, got profits on USDCHF (100pips - demo), GBPUSD (246pips - live), EURUSD (100pips - demo), USDCAD (100pips -demo).

My observations re Sunday (Monday Asia) are that in most cases, the price continues with what it was doing on Friday.

All last week we had huge long runs against the US$, so it's no surprise that a retracement or reversal was imminent.

And I've also noticed that the majority of reversals or big moves, happen at the 8 am EST NY open.  Check a 4 hour chart and you'll see that the 8 am candle is the big one.  The next biggest one is the London open at 4 am EST.  There are other turnaround points, but none as big and consistent as the 8 am NY open.  Open a 4 hour chart and check the past history to confirm it.

That's what happened this morning on all the major pairs.  I believe the GBP/USD will continue to drop at least to a 38% Fibo retracement point @ around 1.4600.

I have added a few indicators to help the fbTemplate with your exit strategy. Attached is a screenshot of the indicators. When I have a confirmation of the three indicators all showing trend change I will exit my trades.

All three must be in agreement.

Short Exit

MTF CCI 14 - exit when 4 hour changes to +100 positive.

THV Trend - when trend color changes to yellow

10tionreader - when 4hr changes to yellow on all three bars

Long Exit

MTF CCI 14 - exit when 4 hour changes to -100 negative

THV Trend - when trend color changes to yellow

10tionreader - when 4hr changes to yellow on all three bars

I am backtesting this and live demo testing this and will post my feedback. The idea is to have a good confirmation that the trend is changing.

Ok...I am thinking about giving a trendline as an area to control wether the EA still trade or not, for better understanding I think u guys should watch this video first (or maybe u watch it already)

http://www.forexbrace.com/content/view/187/77/

Let me give u an example on the daily chart below,

On a short trade or in a downtrend market u draw the trendline to give the EA an area to trade or not (to make it easy, draw the trendline on daily chart and of course after that switch it to 5 Min coz the EA will work on 5 Min chart),

if the price breaks the trendline or entering the forbidden area or above the trendline, the EA will not open another short trade untill we adjust it again and vice versa, so that we dont have to worry about drawdown when the price reverse and we might reduse the SL accordingly. --- 帖子 #1110 ---
I Samurai, i have finally incorporate your idea with Namrettik idea.

This EA allow you to disactivate the trade if the Heiken Ashi is agains your driving condition (If Manage_Trade is = true).  It will also stop all trading if it break the Trend line that you have manually draw on the Chart(if TrendAnalysis is true).  Those features can be activated or disactivated by the EA property in the input folder.

To activate the Trend analysis, you need to establish a Trend line and you need to give it a description with the following format:

...XXXXX...YYYYY_ZZ

XX is for a trend line name (could be nothing)

YYYY need to be Alert (if you want the alert to be activated)

_  This caracter is required

ZZ The amount of pip that you want to have this alert activated

EX.  My trendline Alert_20

This description of the trend line will activate an alert when price is in the range of 20 pip of your trend  line.  If you set up variable emailalert at true in the trendline analysis section of the EA input it will send you an email, Same for the popup variable.

To set this trendline description you need to double clic on the trendline, then right clic while having your cursor on the trend line, you will see a popup window with trendline properties, clic on trendline properties, you will have the popup window with the description field blank. Double clic on the description field and enter your alert as described above.

Once the trend line alert is triggered by price actions, the EA will not generate new trade anymore but will continue to monitor your open trades.  To reset your EA, you need to enter into the EA property (F7) window and clic OK.

One more thing.  With this version you don't need to have the 5 min chart display(you should not if you want to have a meaningfull trend).  Select the timeframe on which you want to place your trendline and trace it.

For those of you who want to trade on an other timeframe than 5 min, you need to change the variable Chart_Time_Frame in the EA properties at the section for FireBird.

Hope their is no bugs in the code.  Test it and let me know

I encourage people to let us know what will be the best parameters to produce positive Pips.

Have a good evening to all.

ActionPl

--- 帖子 #1112 ---
Hi Samurai,

I think your smtp server for yahoomail can be googled, while the username is your userid and password is ur password.

Regarding this EA, when you drive short on aug 2008 it gets 3094 pips while the close - start of the trend shows 1067 pips because it opens new positions on the daily trend every 30-40 pips along the short trend. This means you are gaining pips exponentially rather than linearly. Is this correct? So assuming this is how it works, why do we need to complicate things and turn the EA off when the daily trend shows us it changed. It is easy to just reverse the condition and drive your shorts to longs automatically in code. Just do buys instead of calls and vice versa. I already did this in the EA and am testing it.

This is how I think it works, looking at the code:

start()

1) make sure orders < maxorders

2) Setup Pipstep

3) Check divergence < divergencelimit (why do we need this????)

4) Enter position

- this is the interesting part ( it checks moving avg and RVI to see if its a BUY or SELL, unless you set flag to ONLY BUYS or ONLY SELLS. And it only buys and sells every Pipstep Pips.

5) KeepTrackOfStopLoss(averageopeningprice)

These are the comments from the code on this step:

"

//----------------------- KEEP TRACK OF STOPLOSS TO AVOID RUNAWAY MARKETS

// Sometimes the market keeps trending so strongly the system never reaches it's target.

// This means huge drawdown. After stopping out it falls in the same trap over and over.

// The code below avoids this by only accepting a signal in teh opposite direction after a SL was hit.

// After that all signals are taken again. Luckily this seems to happen rarely.

"

- I'm not sure why we need this if we are only driving one way(can we delete this function?)

So what I did was between step 3 and 4 I checked with the trend indicator running on the daily chart to see if the trend is long or short then place all orders and buys and sells respectively every Pipstep Pips. This would basically allow it to run without interference EXCEPT for sideway trends, if the trend isn't Pipstep Pips big, then it will retrace and you will lose that money most likely. We can handle that if we can detect sideways trends from the trend indicator, or say after 2 stop losses just wait until we get to a trend that passes the Pipstep barrier then place your orders every Pipstep Pips.

Maybe I am misunderstanding the code, but this is what I get from it. The way you are driving it, it's not really Firebird but a manual EA that just places orders every Pipstep (40 Pips) in the direction of the trend you manually set.

Jag

--- 帖子 #1115 ---
gasgas:

Well it seems to be a test between moving averages. In any case the test usually passes so it is has minimal effect.

Two things I think can improve on the EA:

-Start with lower T/P, so that it builds up as more orders come in every Pipstep. Idea is to have carry momentum forward (snowball effect). This will allow you to save money during non-trending times as you won't spend as much by the time you get to the peak and the trend changes.

-When the trend changes, cancel all orders. Most likely you are going to get a Stop loss anyways. This really depends on a good trend indicator, and if your indicator is set to HA indicator is set to daily with 1/2 settings its usually pretty good.

-Automatically switch between long/short version of this EA

I think this will allow you to atleast break even on non trending but make a bigger profit on large up/down trends. I am working on modifying the EA to test for these heuristics.

Jag

--- 帖子 #1117 ---
Hi, i have add some new features on this version vs1_1.

Now you can have the EA waiting for a pattern that you draw on the chart with trend lines.  When price action will hit your trend line, it will start to trade normally. If it reverse and hit a second trend line it will stop trading as version vs1.

You can activate this trend watch feature by having variable TrendLine_watch set to true.

An other feature is you can have your stoploss reduce by a factor when the trendline is hit after trading normally.  So if you set variable "Reduce_factor" at something different than zero, it will divide your stoploss value by the amount that you have enter.  Ex.  A stoploss of 3000 will become 1500 on a 5 digit broker.

Also this version have setup for a 5 digit broker.

Those feature should help us to have more free time and not look at the screen for pattern.  So we can plan to enter trading when a specific pattern will be in place.  So if it happen overnight, we will not miss it.

P.S.  When we do this kind of pattern watching, we should have the EA ready to go long or short, at our next check, we can change it to the way we think it will for the next trend.

Have fun testing it.  Hoppefully it will bring more pips to our accounts.

Bye

Actionpl

--- 帖子 #1128 ---
Hi Samurai, Thanks for your testing, you have found a bug in the programmation. The bug was associated with variable "Manage_trade". When this variable was set to false there was no trade with version 1_1.

Hi shisuyu, I have also check the code for time setting and  those function were not working since the code was using a obsolete function call.

So now in this new version, it is fixed.  You have two way to control the execution of the EA,

First, you can set Variable "TradeFromx and TradeUntilX" for a specific hour.

(Server time not your local time)

Ex.  "TradeFrom1=0" and TradeUntil1=5" This will enable your EA to trade from 0hr 0 min to 5hr 59 min.  You can specify 4 time frame with those variables.  Make sure they are mutually exclusive. If not, you will end up with the minimum hour to the max hour of the day.  Assuming that your server is at GMT hour.  If your server is at Tokio time zone, the hour you enter will be the Tokio time.

The second Parameters are GMT, DST,OpenningHour and ClosingHour.  This will do the same fonction than the previous paragrah but it allow you to enter you local time in the OpenningHour and ClosingHour as long as you have setup the right GMT offset at variable GMT and if you are on Day saving Time you need to put 1 or 0 at variable DST.

So in summary, you have 5 ways to select the trading window.

Your top left scren will show "Bad hour" with the OpenningHour et ClosingHour and trade disable with the "TradeFrom and TradeUntil" variables.

So i have fix the program and now the version 1_2 fix both problem.  None trading situation and the Time setup.

Bye

--- 帖子 #1133 ---
Hi, on a 4 digit broker you need to setup your variable to the # of pip that you are interested to trade on a 5 digit broker you need so multiply those value by 10.

Ex.  Pipstep 40 for 4 digit broler et 400 for the 5 digit.

In version 1_2 i have regroup those variables together this is my setup for a 5 digits broker.

slip = 100;

SafeArea = 400;

PipStep = 250;

TakeProfit = 500;

Stoploss = 3000;

the 4 digits will be

slip = 10;

SafeArea = 40;

PipStep = 25;

TakeProfit = 50;

Stoploss = 300;

Bye

--- 帖子 #1134 ---
Hi Samurai, on your first question here the answer:

If you set up your EA with TrendAnalysis at true and TrendLine_watch at false, The EA will trade in the direction that we want irregardless of the trend line.  So it is where you put your trend line that will make the difference.  The trend line in your picture will do exactly what you have described.  Trade above and stop trading if price action go below.  If your place your trend line above the price action and you think that the market will go down, The EA will trade according to your setup up to the point it hit the trend line in case of a reverse action.

IF variable Trendline_watch is set at true, The EA will not trade up to a point where the price action will hit a trendline with an alert setup.  At this point, it will start to trade as if the Trendline_watch was set to false.

For your question two, i need to compare the code of version 63G and 63H.

I will let you know. It will take more time.

Bye

Hi Samurai,

i have look at the trigger mechanisim and version H have a concept of save area to trade, it adding the BullsPower with the Bearspower indicator as this

Safe1 = iBullsPower(NULL,PERIOD_M15,20,6,0)+iBearsPower(NULL,PERIOD_M15,20,6,0);

If this somme of those two indicators fall inside the SaveArea variable, it allow the trade.  So if you want to simulate more closely the G version change this parameter for a bigger number as 5000 and try it.

--- 帖子 #1146 ---
Hi to all, Divyendu, this version can do pratically what you have proposed in customizing the variables.

Vs 1.3 include a Trailing Stop feature.  For those of you who want to use it.

This feature does not work well in a none trending market.  You need to have trend with a slope of at least 30 degree according to my experience.

It work this way:  If variable "TrailingStopFlag" is set at true, the EA will analyse your trade and switch from Stoploss to a trailing stop when the following condition is met: If the trade is at "TStrigger" pips from your "TakeProfit" value, it will switch to a trailing stop according to variable "TrailingStop".

The other feature that will do most of what Divyendu is proposing is the following:

If variable "TrendAnalysis" and "ChangeOrder" are true, when the treend line with an Alert is hit, it will reduce the stoploss by a factor equivalent to what is in variable "Reduce_Factor"  Exemple.  You have a stop loss of 3000 and the trendline is hit.  At the next tic, the Stoploss will be reduce to 1500 if you have set variable "Reduce_Factor" to 2.  So, during the trading scession, we place a first trend line and wait, if it is hit, it will reduce your stop loss according to variable Reduce_factor. At this time this variable may be set at 2, it allow more freedom to the price action.  At that point you can draw an other trend line (like Divyendu propose for his close) but this time you change the Reduce_factor to 20.  So what will happen, the EA will place the stoploss at "slip" point away from the market. Variable "slip" is in the the Firebird section. The default value of "slip" is 100, if you put it to tight, the modify order will be rejected in high volatility price action.

Also in this version i have fix the problem associate to changing the time period while it was trading.  So now you can do whatever you want with the chart and the EA is still using the chart time period describe in variable "Chart_Time_frame".

The last change is in the Status of the EA in Yellow at top of the screen, it represent the choice that you have made in the TrendAnalysis section.

Lastly: here the setup summary for different configuration

For vs G emulation.

Set all variables to false for TrendAnalysis, ManageTrade, TrailingStop and set variable "safearea" at 10,000.

For Vs H03:  Set all variables to false for TrendAnalysis, ManageTrade and TrailingStop.

If you don't want to take any trade if the Heiken Ashi is agains your prevision set variable "manage_Trade" at true.

To activate Trend Analysis, set your variable "TrendAnalysis" at true.

Look at post of v1.1 and 1.2 to have more detail of how it work.

P.S.  Make sure to set the description of your trend line as described in previous post in order to have this feature work.  Also, once a trend line is hit, the Description is reset to remove the Alarm setup and you need to reinitialise the EA to get out of the "Broken trend" state.

Now we have a EA with an autopilot and alarms.  As Samurai is saying, it should provide us with more free time and less preoccupation about what is happening on the market.  But you need to look at your chart twice a day in order to do the adjusment required and optimize your trading strategy.

I did test those features and everything seem to work as plan.  I count on you guys to test it even further in order to get all the bugs out.

Have a good trading week.

Actionpl
