--- 帖子 #1159 ---
Hi Divyendu,  yes the magic# is created automatically using this formula

int MagicNumber=0;

for (int i=0; i<5; i++)

{

MagicNumber=MagicNumber*3+StringGetChar(Symbol(),i);

}

MagicNumber=MagicNumber*3+Chart_Time_Frame;

return(MagicNumber);

So if is fonction of the symbol and the variable Chart_Time_Frame.

Will the EA ignore manual trades on the same chart?

Yes, unless you giveit a magic# that meet  the formula above.

Bye

Answer: Your understanding is right. If you want to force a trade in a rapid changing environment as today, you need to increase the "SaveArea" variable in the Firebird section.

My understanding is with trendAnalysis set to true it will stop trading when the trendline that I draw that has an alert set will stop trading when it hit that line. YES

Answer: With this variable set at true, the EA will wait to hit a trend line with an alert before starting to trade.  Then it will act as if the Trendline_watch variable was set to false.

Manage_trade = T does this setting work the same was as Trendanalysis except that it is triggered by the Heiken Ashi Candle only.
No, Manage_Trade will do exactly what you have requested.  It will prevent a trade in the direction agains your choice. according to Heiken Ashi indicator.  Ex. It will trade only short if the candle is red. You can select on which time frame you want this indicator and you can select which candle you want to monitor by changing variable "Index".  If you select the current candle, use 0.  But make sure to set your email variable to false if you select the current candle. If you want the previous candle set it to 1.

Hope this clarify how this work.

--- 帖子 #1176 ---
This message appear when you doing live trading and that the trade that you have is generating a high rate of loss.  Variable "PippsLoss" will affect this message.  IF you increase this variable, it mean that you can manage a higher rate of loss.  It is a warning that your account is going in the wrong direction.  If you don't want to see that set your variable "writelog" at 0,

--- 帖子 #1184 ---
Hi Samurai,

in order to get a good understanding of how this EA work with trend line do the following.

1- Set your EA as describ in your post

2- Set your chart on a timeperiod of 1 minutes

3- Draw a trend line very close above and below the current price action

4- Draw a horizontal trend line below(or above) the current price action

5- Set the Alert in the description box as shown below(picture)

6- Wait for the Price Action to break on of the trend line

You should see in the upper left corner the message Trend broken

7- Look at the description of the trend line that have been broken, the description will have been change and they is no more an alert associate to it.

8- To restart the trading, you need to go in EA property and clic on OK.

9- continue testing by adding an alert to the trend line that was broken

bye

Hi Divyendu,  make sure to have those variables set like as follow to disable the bad hour message

GMT = 0

DST = 0

OpeningHour = 0

ClosingHour = 24

To make sure that you are not going to have "Trade disable" message due to time, set the folowing variables this way:

TradeFrom1 = 0

TradeUntil1 = 24

In order to desactivate the high volatility market verification set variable:

SafeArea= 10000

This should solve your irration.

--- 帖子 #1200 ---
Hi to all, i have made some modification to prevent the instabillity problem identivied by Samurai and Namrettik. I have not found any bugs but have change the logic in order to be more robust in time where the price action are rapidly changing.  So take note of the following.

1- When placing an alert on your trend, Make sure to have a Capital letter as your first letter of the alarm.  Ex.  Alarm_30.  If it is not written this way, the EA will not take action on your trend. I recommend a minimum of 30 for a 5 digits broker et 3 pip for the 4 digits broker.

2- I have made the comments on the top left side more meaninfull. It will help you to adjust "SaveArea" and "DivergenceLimit" variables.  Those two variables are use to filter trade when the price action is too volatile.  If you want to increase your risk level and have more trade adjust those variables according to the message that you will see. Message: "SaveArea too low: 500"  meant that you need to put variable "SafeArea" larger than 500 in order to validate this market condition.

Message "DivergenceLimit too low  = 0.003" it mean that you have to increase variable "DivergenceLimit" in order to accept this market condition.

I have validate on my system in foward testing mode and it is stable for friday market conditions.  I have tested all alerts conditions with popup and email, everything is working on my system.  Check it out and let me know what kind of error message that your are getting.

Samurai and Nam, if you find again a trade after the trend have been broken, provide me a print screen of your chart and a print screen of the folder "Experts" in metatrader.

P.S.  make sure to not change the time frame of your chart since changing time frame will reinitialize the EA.

P.S.2 Changing time period of your chart is an other way to get the EA out of the condition TrendLine Broken and start trading again.

P.S.3 If you have multiple trend line with Alarm_xx the EA will toggle between active trading and disable trading each time it hit a trend with an Alarm_xx.  This could be use for more elaborate trading strategy.

Hope this version will be more stable and allow more free time to traders.

Bye

ActionPl

--- 帖子 #1211 ---
Hi ayoneeyee, whatever the chart you are placing the EA it will have the same results since it is not fonction of the timeperiod that is on your chart.

This allow you to draw your trend line on any time period.

If you want to change the time period that you want to place the EA on, you need to change the following variable "Chart_Time_Frame" in the FireBird section.  So if you want the EA to take decision base on 30 minutes charts, assign to this variable 30.  ex.  Chart_Time_Frame=30

Hope this clarify your results.

P.S.  Remember, you will have to fine tune all the other parameters that have been setup on the EA for 5 min.  Try it and let us know your results.

bye

ActionPl.

--- 帖子 #1241 ---
Hi guys.

I did some testing of EuroUsd, and this is what I came up with:

The cross is a good deal more volatile than any time before the middle of 2008, and it is possible the earning potential of Firebird will be enhanced by a wider stop loss margin.

On the picture you can see two envelopes: the blue one is related to Low, shift 1, deviation 4% (which represents 540 pips). The red one is related to High, with the same settings. As you can see this period since Dec 08 to the present day has only triggered this 540 pip SL five times. A SL of 300 pips would have been triggered many many more times, due to the volatility.

Samuraj kindly explained his settings and mentioned he estimates 400 pips gain per day in an unbroken trend, and a 500 pip hit when the trend breaks, based on trendline automatic stop. For my earnings potential calculation I have used 300 pips gain per day and a 870 pip hit when trend reverses. I have used the simplest most automatic method of reversing the driving of Firebird (No need for complicated positioning of trend-lines). If during any day a SL is hit all trades are cancelled and the next day trades in the opposite direction are started.  No thinking is required for this, just a mechanical application of this change over when a stop loss is hit (Can be done with the automated trend-line, by putting it where SL is likely to be hit).

Starting with $2500, and compounding all the interest, it seems as if it is possible to reach $25000 in less than a year ( I have real data from Dec 2008, and have extrapolated future figures on these.)

Please tell me my calculation is correct

D

--- 帖子 #1244 ---
Hi Okehiedon

Congratulations on your good results on the GU.

Yes the ATR on the Eurodollar is as you say less than my numbers. Let me explain:

These musings of mine are in the context of Samurajpower's and Actionpl's recent work with dynamic trendline recognition to help run the EA.

Let's say that you are 'driving' firebird long; allowing it only to take long positions in a (Daily Chart) Uptrend.

The highest position possible for the day is somewhere below the high price of the day (25  to 50 pips below? here is something for somebody to research).

For the stop loss of that highest position to be triggered its TakeProfit must not be triggered, and the price must fall the entire length of its stop loss (300 is commonly used at the moment).

I find 300pips SL will be triggered quite often due to large retracements of the EuroUsd - retracements that still do not change the overall trend.

What I have described is not really an Average Range in the ordinary sense. I have described a space large enough to accommodate large retracements that did not constitute trend changes. To do this I have used two 'envelope' indicators.

One envelope (timeframeay, period:1) based on the low of the day indicates how high the price can go before that lowest position is tripped and the other, based on the high of the day, is the same but reverse.

Hope this clarifies my previous post

D

--- 帖子 #1245 ---
Hi, In version 1_3b, a function read in the object description if there is an Alert set, it will trig when the price go below or upper the trend which you have trace.  In Version 1_3a, it is a window around the trend line define by the number of pip identified by "Alert_30". In this case the window was 3 pips for a 5 digit broker. That is why it is not safe for large tic to tic variations.

Features of Version 1.4 are not ready it will require more testing and debug to make it usable and userfriendly.  The idea is to use what we are going to place in the trendline description to tell the EA to buy or sell.

Ex.  If you place the following description: "DownTrend_Trade_Alert_50" The EA will stop any further entry after crossing the trend line and will initiate a special trade (buy) after price goes above 5 pips from the trend line.

This will should reduce our drawdown. Assuming that it is a real trend reversal.  Obviously you will still need to drive your system in a semi-automatic mode and do manual adjustment if it was not a real reversal.

Bye

So idea is to hedge the position if it is 50pips(5 digit) or 5 pips (4 digit) above the trend line and there is no more window?  Yes, You will be able to select any window that you like.

What happens when the trend line is broken (special order is executed) Yes and then price comes back under the trend line? It should not execute orders under normal conditions right? Right This would cause problems if it did since if trend line is crossed, chances are a new resistance has been set and it will cross the trend line again, which will cause you to lose money on the hedged (special order) position. Your righ again. That why it is a semi-automatic system.  This process will give us more time to react and adjust to the new trend by closing trade or whatever you want.  Overall it should reduce our drawdown.

--- 帖子 #1266 ---
Hi, it all depend of your selection.  If you select true for Manage_Trade, it will do a trade only in the same direction than your Heiken Ashi indicator.

I believe that its initial function was to stop trade after color changed, right? Yes and No, it will disable the trade only during time where price action is agains your setup. Ex. Manage_Trade=true, Heiken_Ashi_timeperiod=240 and index=1, it will prevent a trade if the previous bar is agains your position seting.  If you drive long, it will take trade only during white bars.
is that function still applicable in v1.3a and up?. Yes

Look at the first chart below, divided by column A, B and C.

This is an explanation pic of general idea of Firebird EA with trendline combined.

On Column A

It was a downtrend (Drive Short Only) and the trendline devide between the trade area and not trade area, when the price touch and break the trendline the EA will devide the SL on the opening position by the Reduce_factor variable and then the EA will stop untill we activate the EA again. See the circle No.1

Its the same on column B and C depends on trend direction.

Look at the second chart.

That is a sample of trade I take untill now, on 29 April the arrow and and HA is in line showing an uptrend move (see the first white circle), and the previous candle shows pressure on downtrend to go up so I took "Long Only" mode, currently I gained +1300pips and keep moving. I lock the profit with trendline becouse when the price go down and touch the trendline then the EA will close opening position, if I put the trendline correctly then I will loss for only -300pips (see the 2nd white circle I draw), and I still got at least +1000pips in my bank right now. If the price keep moving up then I will keep gaining green pips, but if it goes down i will only loss arround -300pips (not much I guess). I only adjust the trendkine once a day, I dont trade news, I can still do other thing and have fun enjoying my life (mhmm ..I guess trading is so easy...). Unlike a fully automatic EA, doing this way the control is in our hand 100%, Keep pipin' guys.....

--- 帖子 #1291 ---
Ok, thanks gasgas for the Stochastic Divergence indicator. I'm using this, plus another one for crosses that catches major trends.

So basically it's samurai power's chart, plus the QQE indicator I use and the Stochastic Divergence.

I made a zip file, with the chart template.tpl and all the indicators you need to make it easier for everyone. Attached an image too that explains.

I'll sum up the rules for my chart:
1) Watch for an arrow on the chart.

2) Check the Stochastic Divergence indicator for the cross.
3) The QQE indicator direction has to confirm the trend. A cross of the red dotted line or a 50 line cross. The QQE will not confirm smaller crosses as the Stochastic Divergence does, however the system will get the needed pips even with smaller crosses if we enter immediately after the arrow/stochastic cross without waiting for 1 candle to close..

As you can see the Stochastic Divergence indicator catches more swing trades (check the picture), while the QQE is a strong trend indicator that can help you draw trend lines and get the direction on long term, 1 week or more.

If you set variable TrendLineWatch to true, the system will not trade up to a point where the price action hit a trend with an Alert set to it.  So if the pair does not trend, you can set two trend on up and one down with Alert to it.  When one of those will be hit the system will start to trade the way you have selected.  This is a nice feature to setup your chart and you don't have to look at it every hour or so.

So if you don't want to wait for a trend to be broken before it start to trade leave this variable to false.

Bye

ActionPL

--- 帖子 #1317 ---
If you set manage trade to true, the EA will look at variable "index" and if it is set at 1, it will trade or not according to the previous bar setup to the timeframe that you have selected on Heiken_Ashi_timeperiod.  So to monitor what happen, you need to set your chart to the same time frame that you have set in your setup.  And look at the Heiken Ashi indicator.

P.S.  if you set index to 0, it will look at the current bar, so if the bar change color during the 240min, you can have a trade if it is in line with the trade direction that you want.

Bye

Actionpl

--- 帖子 #1330 ---
Hi! all. My biggest problem is not the point of entry, it is when to get out of the trade without giving back what i had.

Heiken Ashi is for me a nice tool that help me to trail my Stops and maximize my profits without or less fear and greed (give the price a chance to get there).

In fact its kind of a dynamic SL: It will move the SL 1 or 2 pips on a HACandle and the next bar, the SL could move 6 to 7 pip or more. Its better then a static 20 pips trailing stop that you are sure to lose 20 pips at the end.

Here are some setting for externs variables (subjective).

Hardstop = (40) pip   // Initial SL when the trade is open

MoveToBE = (20) pip   // Will move the SL to BE if the trade have reach (x) pip but is still in opposite color

TakeProfit1 = (40) pip   // Take first profit at (x) pip

TakeProfit2 = (60) pip   // Take second profit at (x) pip

TakeProfit3 = (80) pip   // Take Third profit at (x) pip

TakeProfit4 = break of the trailing step HA (close all remaining)

PercentClose1 = (25) % // Close (x) % of the trade after first TakeProfit1 is reach

PercentClose2 = (25) % // Close (x) % of the trade after second TakeProfit2 is reach

PercentClose3 = (25) % // Close (x) % of the trade after third TakeProfit3 is reach

TrailspikeCond = True  // Will allow TrailSpike

TrailSpike = (10) pip    // will trail from the current candle: if price went (x) pip of current HACandle... (close all)

TrailspikePip = (5) pip    // Will trail (x) pip from the current candle (ex: trail by 5 pips STEP)

In a SELL: When the EA find a range of 10 pips between the current low of the HACandle et the actual price

it will start the trail of 5 pips.

CloseAll = true                                 // if true, will Close All position at the condition (HACandle open opposite color)

not if the HardStop is still on

HACandleTimeFrame = (15)M              // Will Look at HACandle the (x) timeFrame only.

TrailFromXPrevCandle = (1) candle      // Will trail from (x) HACandle (default = 1) (will look at the previous HACandle)

PutStopXPipFromHA = (2) pip             // Will trail from (x) pip of the TrailFromXPrevCandle (default = 2)

(scenario)

A trade is open: SELL

1. The trade is place on Green HACandle, so the HardStop is place at 20 pips.

2. Then the price move 12 pips in our favor, but the HACandle is still Green. The SL is then put to BE.

3. In the same HACandle the price cross our first TakeProfit1(20pips), so it close 25% of the position.

4. Three Candle later the HACandle close Red, So the SL is move at the high + PutStopXPipFromHA(2 pips).

5. In the same candle the price reach our TakeProfit2. So it close 25% of the trade.

6. The next Candle, the SL is move again at the previous high + PutStopXPipFromHA(2 pips).

In the same Candle the price reach the TakeProfit3... So it close 25% of the trade.

7. We are lucky the price still go in our favor and we reach a little spike(yellow bar). So the Trailing Stop(5pips) is on

20 pips later it Close All remaining position. in this case is the last 25% of the position. ( the chart was edited for the purpuse of the scenario)

PS: I know that the HACandle are always in motion.. But when the EA find a 10 pips between the current HACandle and the actual price...

It Trigger the Trailing Stop.

Attached Image
Attached Image

TakeOTW

--- 帖子 #1333 ---
Hi to all, with version 1.4, this fonctionnality will be included.

By the way, you can have as many trend line with alert as you want.  The EA will toogle between able to trade and unable to trade each time it hit a trend line with an "Alert_" attach to it.  So be careful with what you are doing.

It should work this way.

If you put the following description in your trend line: DownTrend_Close_Alert_

As soon the price action will go above the trend line, it will close all sell open  trade if it is a DownTrend.  If you put as description UpTrend_Close_Alert_  all buy open trade will be close.

This will version will also included the trade hedging fonction as described in previous post.

If the description is: DownTrend_Trade_Alert_20  it will initiate a buy trade when the price action will be 20 pips above your trend line. As soon the price action will go above your trend line, it reduce the stoplost by the factor that you have given in the "Reduce_factor" variable. Same fontionnality for the UpTrend but with a sell trade.

I hope i don't confuse people with all those features.  For those of you who take time to understand it, it allow you to plan the execution of your strategy whithout being in front of your screen waiting for something to happen.

Bye

P.S.  I will release vs 1.4 for Sunday openning.  I still have some test to do in simulation.

--- 帖子 #1356 ---
Hi, i have completed my test on this version for those two new features.

A trend line with the following word "Close_" will act as described in my previous post(just clic on the blue arrow at the beginning of this post to get the details).  And a trend line with "Trade_" in it will intiate a hedge trade when the trend line is hit.

Note: If the Trendline with a Close in it is hit, the EA will stop trading waiting for your intervention.  Any other trendline that is hit will toogle the EA state between able to trade and unable to trade.

This should provide us with more free time and still monitor the market efficiently.

Bye

Actionpl

--- 帖子 #1369 ---
A "close" in the trendline will stop the EA from any new positions in the same direction and reduce the stoploss by the reduction factor.

Manage trades will use the HA to do automated trading in both directions. If HA is long it will set EA to long and vice versa. Keep Manage_trades to false if you want to use the EA with the trendlines we are discussing.

Jag

--- 帖子 #1372 ---
Hi Serge,

here my answer in blue
Say I have a downtrend, draw my trendline and in the description type Downtrend_Close_Alert_10 and say I have my Reduce_factor set to 2.

What is the effect of this? Will it close my order when it is within 10 pips of my trendline or just cut my stoploss in half?
With this setup, the EA will close all your trade (sell) and stop the EA to take any new trade when the price will go above the trendline. It does not take into account variable Reduce_factor when you have "Close_" in your description.  It does not take into account the number you put at the end also.
If you want to work with the "Reduce_factor" and have the EA manage the close, write your description this way. "DownTrend_Alert_10".  This way, when the price go above the Trend, it will change your Stop loss by reducing it by a factor of 2 if the variable "Reduce_factor" is at 2 and stop the EA to take new trade waiting for your decision.

P.S.  Again, the number at the end of "Alert_xx" is not used.  The number at the end of the "Alert_"  is take into account if you have only "Alert_xx" in your description or if you have "Trade_" in your description in conjonction with "DownTrend_" or "UpTrend_".

I was also wondering if I am understanding the Heiken_Ashi_timeperiod setting correctly? If you have Manage_Trade set to "true" and Heiken_Ashi_timeperiod set to 1440 (daily) when the daily HA changes colour I am assuming it just turns off the EA not allowing any more trades?
If you have Manage_Trade at true, it will allow trade only in the direction of the previous daily bar if variable "index" is at 1 or the current bar if the "index" is at 0. Be careful about index being at 0, since the current bar can switch color many time during a given day.  You can used this feature with any of the other features of the EA.

Bye

--- 帖子 #1373 ---
No, you can not open a trade manually for testing since the EA will not recognize your trade.

The way to do it is to force the trade to open by using the trendline with "Trade_" in the description.

let say you want to open a buy, do the fowllowing. (Will work only with version 1.4)

1-Trace a trend line below the price action

2- Give it the following description, "DownTrend_Trade_Alert_01"

3- As soon you will clic ok and a new tic come in, it should open a buy

then you can change the description of your trend line to test whatever you want.

You can also used the simulator to test it.  Do CTRL-R on your metatrader and follow the instruction.

--- 帖子 #1381 ---
Hi ayoneeyee,

What is this function actually going to do? is it going to open a trade in the opposite direction while the other trade is on Yes, that the intend if you put in your trendline "Trade_" or it will close initial trade and open another in the opposite? Yes it can do that as well if you put in your description "Close_Trade_"  Ex. DownTrend_Close_Trade_Alert_50

this description will make the EA to close all sell trades as soon it goes above the trendline and it will take a buy if the price goes at 5 pip above it (5 digits broker).

It is quite flexible as it is now.  With version 1.5 it will be even easier since we will only pay attention to how we draw the trend and what we want to do when price hit the trend.

bye

--- 帖子 #1396 ---
I am trying to put together a master sheet that describes all the EA settings and Functions.  I have many of them completed, but some I do not understand.  Can anyone who knows the definition of these please fill them in below and I will put it all together and post it here..  Thanks

EA SETTINGS:
TrendAnalysis:  I think this is the master switch to enable the trendlines…????????????????

TrendLineWatch: If you set variable TrendLineWatch to true, the system will not trade up to a point where the price action hit a trend with an Alert set to it. So if the pair does not trend, you can set two trend on up and one down with Alert to it. When one of those will be hit the system will start to trade the way you have selected. This is a nice feature to setup your chart and you don't have to look at it every hour or so.

So if you don't want to wait for a trend to be broken before it start to trade leave this variable to false.
ChangeOrder:  ???
Reduce_Factor:  Used when Trend_Watch is set to False. If set at 0, the stoploss will not be changed.  If set any number other than 0, the stoploss will be reduced by this factor.
Example:  If in a downtrend and price rises to the DownTrend_Alert_  trendline, the stopploss value will be changed to ( current stoploss / Reduce_Factor).  So if your current stoploss is 100, and your Reduce_Factor is 2, if the trendline is hit it will be changed to 50 (100/2).

Manage_Trade:  if set at TRUE: it will only allow trade in the Heiken Ashi direction.

Heiken Ahsi Timeperiod :  variable sets the timeperiod used for the Heiken Ashi direction.  (1440=Daily, 240=H4, 60=H1…)

Index:  If variable "index" is at 1 it looks at previous bar,  or the current bar if the "index" is at 0. Be careful about index being at 0, since the current bar can switch color many times during a given day. You can use this feature with any of the other features of the EA.

Chart_Time_Frame:  TimeFrame for default indicators
MA_length:  Firebird calculates a Simple Moving Average of this length ( 10 default), and then shifts it up and down by the Percent Variable (2% default) to form a channel.
MA_Timeframe:   Timeframe for the moving average above, in minutes.
MAtpe:  0=close, 1=HL (manage trade or trend analysis will not work with Matype=1)
Percent:  the percentage amount to shift the MA bands to form the channel described above.
TradeOnFriday:  >0 trades on friday
Slip:  exits only
Lots:  The size of the lot you will be trading.
MaxOpenOrders:  Maximum number of positions to have open simultaneously
SafeArea:  ???
PipStep:  if position goes this amount of pips against you add another.
TakeProfit:  Amount of profit in Pips to exit position
StopLoss:  total loss on all open positions in pips
TrailingStopFlag:  ???
TrailingStop:  trailling stop value, order will be modified at BID or ADK ±TrailingStop
TStrigger:  Once the price hits ( TakeProfit – Tstrigger ), it cancels Ttakeprofit and puts a trailing stop.
MinMarginLevel:  Below this Minimum Margin Level percent % trading stops
TradeFrom1:  Place trades "From" - "Until"
TradeUntil2:  Place trades "From" - "Until"
Fast_Period:  ????
Fast_Price:  ???
Slow_Period:   ???
Slow_Price:   ???
DivergenceLimit:  ???
Use_V63D_Divergence:  0 = Use original method for divergence, 1 = use in iFXAnalyzer
IncreasementType:  0=just add every PipStep,  >0 =OrdersTotal()^x *Pipstep  ????????????????
DVLimit: :  ???
PipsGoal: :  ???
PipsLoss: ???
GMT:  Your Brokers time offset from GMT.  For example:  if your brokers time is 23:30 and GMT is 20:30 this setting would be 3.
DST:  0=Standard 1=Daylight Saving
OpeningHour: ???
ClosingHour: ???
Writelog: ???

--- 帖子 #1397 ---
Hi, Sergiel

When I have a trendline described as "Downtrend_Close_Alert_" what is happening is that when the line is breached any existing short trade has its stop loss value reduced by the Reduce_Factor (ie. Reduce_Factor = 2)

No trades are closed and the EA is not deactivated but continues to open new short positions above the trendline.
You have to pay attention to the spelling.  Your trend description should have been: "DownTrend_Close_Alert_"  Each word have to start with a Capital letter.  Down, Up, Close, Trade, Alert  and be follow with "_" caracter.  So in your description you did not have the Capital Letter  on Trend so it did act on this description as it was only an Alert_00.  So by having 0 as the window, in fact you did not have any space to take action that why it did not took action.  That is why i recommend to put at least 40 for a 5 digit broker when you use only the Alert_xx trend line.  Hope this is clear.  So retry with a capital letter at the beginning of each word and it will work.

I also noticed then when my "Downtrend_Close_Alert_" line is breached is removes the Alert_ part within the description. Is this normal? Yes it is normal.  The EA will reset the Alert condition otherwise it will start to osccillate while the price is around the trend line. That why you need to take action and reinitialise the EA after your modification when the trendline have been hit.

Bye

ActionPl

Hi TheGabriel, this is a key factor of the original FireBird. If you disable it, you will prevent to have more than 1 trade activated for a given pair. If it is what you want, you can disable it by having the variable "PipSpep set ot a big number, like 10000.

Good luck.

EA SETTINGS:
TrendAnalysis:  I think this is the master switch to enable the trendlines…????????????????Yes

TrendLineWatch:If you set variable TrendLineWatch to true, the system will not trade up to a point where the price action hit a trend with an Alert set to it. So if the pair does not trend, you can set two trend on up and one down with Alert to it. When one of those will be hit the system will start to trade the way you have selected. This is a nice feature to setup your chart and you don't have to look at it every hour or so.

So if you don't want to wait for a trend to be broken before it start to trade leave this variable to false. Yes, 100% exact
ChangeOrder:  ???It is not needed anymore, i will remove it on the next release.
Reduce_Factor:  Used when Trend_Watch is set to False. If set at 0, the stoploss will not be changed. If set any number other than 0, the stoploss will be reduced by this factor.
Example: If in a downtrend and price rises to the DownTrend_Alert_ trendline, the stopploss value will be changed to ( current stoploss / Reduce_Factor). So if your current stoploss is 100, and your Reduce_Factor is 2, if the trendline is hit it will be changed to 50 (100/2).
Yes, 100% exact

Manage_Trade:  if set at TRUE: it will only allow trade in the Heiken Ashi direction. Yes

Heiken Ahsi Timeperiod:  variable sets the timeperiod used for the Heiken Ashi direction.  (1440=Daily, 240=H4, 60=H1…) Yes

Index:  If variable "index"is at 1 it looks at previous bar,  or the current bar if the "index" is at 0. Be careful about index being at 0, since the current bar can switch color many times during a given day. You can use this feature with any of the other features of the EA. Yes

Chart_Time_Frame:  TimeFrame for default indicators
MA_length:  Firebird calculates a Simple Moving Average of this length ( 10 default), and then shifts it up and down by the Percent Variable (2% default) to form a channel. if price action fall inside this window, it is one of the condition to initiate a trade
MA_Timeframe:   Timeframe for the moving average above, in minutes.
MAtpe:  0=close, 1=HL (manage trade or trend analysis will not work with Matype=1) Right
Percent:  the percentage amount to shift the MA bands to form the channel described above.
TradeOnFriday:  >0 trades on friday
Slip:  exits only Amount of pip allow to slip while closing trades with "Close_" description
Lots:  The size of the lot you will be trading.
MaxOpenOrders:  Maximum number of positions to have open simultaneously
SafeArea:  ??? Filter to prevent trade in volatile time. Small number will prevent trade while price action is moving fast.
PipStep:  if position goes this amount of pips against you add another.
TakeProfit:  Amount of profit in Pips to exit position
StopLoss:  total loss on all open positions in pips
TrailingStopFlag:  ??? to activate the trailling stop function (false no trailling stop)
TrailingStop:  trailling stop value, order will be modified at BID or ADK ±TrailingStop
TStrigger:  Once the price hits ( TakeProfit – Tstrigger ), it cancels Ttakeprofit and puts a trailing stop. Yes
MinMarginLevel:  Below this Minimum Margin Level percent % trading stops No more position will be open
TradeFrom1:  Place trades "From" - "Until"
TradeUntil2:  Place trades "From" - "Until"
Fast_Period:  ???? use in Divergence filter
Fast_Price:  ??? use in Divergence filter
Slow_Period:   ??? use in Divergence filter
Slow_Price:   ??? use in Divergence filter
DivergenceLimit:  ??? rate of change of price have to be less than, it is an other filter to prevent trade in volatile market
Use_V63D_Divergence:  0 = Use original method for divergence, 1 = use in iFXAnalyzer 0 for current bar and 1 for previous bar.
IncreasementType:  0=just add every PipStep,  >0 =OrdersTotal()^x *Pipstep  ????????????????If different than 0, it will adjust variable PipSteps effect in function of the number of trade open and the value of IncreasementType.  (Not tested)
DVLimit: :  ??? Not used
PipsGoal: :  ???Not used
PipsLoss: ??? Use only in live account to warned you that you loosing too much money in relation to your equity
GMT:  Your Brokers time offset from GMT.  For example:  if your brokers time is 23:30 and GMT is 20:30 this setting would be 3.
DST:  0=Standard 1=Daylight Saving
OpeningHour: ???An other way to set the EA trading hour
ClosingHour: ??? "
Writelog: ??? flag to enable to write history of your transaction.  will enable also warning function to warn you if your loosing money too fast in a live account.

--- 帖子 #1413 ---
Hi Andy, the only way the EA will do what it did,  it is because a trend line was active. A trendline is active if it have the following word in the description. "Alert_".  I've noticed that  we can have a lot a hold trendline when we do test and if you don't delete it, it can cause us problems.  I'm working on a solution to clean those old trend line automatically. For now you have to do it manually.

Do the following.

1-left clic inside the chart window

2- Do CTRL+B

3- left clic on the Object colum to sort all objects

4- Delete all trendline by selecting it and clic on delete

5- close this window

6- Save your template using the same name and override the existing one.

7- Retry your test

This way you will clean all trend object that can interfere with your testing and by refreshing your template, they will not come back.

Bye

Actionpl

--- 帖子 #1414 ---

--- 帖子 #1428 ---
You need to adjust the safearea to a higher level and the divergence limit.

My setup is:

SafeArea=10,000  basicaly disable it

DivergenceLimit=0.05

If you look at left top screen you will see message "divergence too low" that mean your setup is too low for the given pair.  you need to find the right setup.  If you put it too high, you will disable those filter and get in market that are moving too fast.  It could be big winner but also traders trap.  Same type of message for SafeArea.

Bye

--- 帖子 #1429 ---
Hi ountalara, If this comment appear and stay there for more than 10 min and you can see price changing and you have communication, it meant that your metatrader pgm is broken.  Unload the program and start it again. Normally you should not see this message for more than a split second.

If you see message marketAnalysis, it is that you are in a waiting time since you had a close in the last 10 min.  The EA will not trade for 10 min after a close. That is a feature from the initial FireBird.

Bye

ActionPl.

--- 帖子 #1430 ---
FireBird will open a trade when

1- If no trade is open, it will open a trade as soon the price go in the window define by your variable "malengh" and "Matimeframe" and Percent. Also you  need to pass the filter condition for SaveArea, and Divergence then you need to have the Relative Vigor index going your way between the current bar and previous bar.

2- it will open trade also if all the previous condition are met and that the price when agains your position by more than "pipstep" if you already have a trade open.

This is quite complex but, in general, it will open trade when market retrace and that the volatility is not too high and you are on the safe side of the trendline and inside the timeperiod that you have setup.

If you want to know exactly how it work, you need to look at the code and understand it.

Bye

--- 帖子 #1431 ---
I've never test it live.  So i have look at the code and could you try the following and let me know.

Set your last variable  "writelog" to 1.

This will produce a file which will follow your equity variation.  If from tic to tic, your equity reduce by more than this operation: "Pipsloss * lots" it will stop openning new trade and you will have message "excessive loss".  It will not close the open trades. So you need to monitor your account.

Bye

Actionpl

--- 帖子 #1448 ---
1- Go on your metatrader menue "insert" then "line" then "trendline"

2- Place your cursor on the chart and clic left and draw your line

3- Double clic on your trendline and right clic on it,

4- On the contex menue left clic on trendline properties

5- Fill the description box on the common tab.

Good luck

Bye

--- 帖子 #1452 ---
There is a divergence limit parameter, by default it is set to 0.002. In the EA, the codes calculate the divergence for every tick and if the divergence is over 0.002 then it will show the "bad hours" message indicating it is not safe to trade.

This message will show up on all JPY pairs very often.

--- 帖子 #1455 ---
Please double check if the GMT and DST are the same on live and demo. But no matter what GMT and DST are, the divergence is over the limit for sure, otherwise you won't receive the message.

If the settings on live and demo are absolutely the same then the only possibility is that the data feeds from live and demo are a bit different. Maybe you are using different brokers or the same broker but provides you with a little bit different data for live and for demo.

BTW, I noticed that if I set Use_V63D_Divergence to true, it opens fewer trades, so I set it to false.

Good luck!

--- 帖子 #1486 ---
When I back test FireBird, I found that if you trade with 0.1 lots, it is easy to get a -$600 drawdown in no more than 3 days (I use 150 pips stop loss, if I use 300 pips I double the loss). But of course it will quickly gain back.

So make sure you have more than $2000 in your account if you want to trade with 0.1 lots.

Another thing I found is very useful is to set Manage_Trade to True, and set Index to 1. This way if the previous 4hr bar is red, the EA will stop trading. That way you may lose some good oppurtunities but you are protected well too.

--- 帖子 #1501 ---
Hi Baby001,

here the code to access to the info from this indicator. Thv3_trend_R is for the Red bar, _G for Green and _Y for Yellow

Thv3_trend_R=iCustom(NULL,Thv3_trend_timeperiod,"Thv3 trend",NULL,0,1);

Thv3_trend_G=iCustom(NULL,Thv3_trend_timeperiod,"Thv3 trend",NULL,1,1);

Thv3_trend_Y=iCustom(NULL,Thv3_trend_timeperiod,"Thv3 trend",NULL,2,1);

Let us know if you your strategy is giving you good results.  My test did not show very good results.

--- 帖子 #1511 ---
Yea Trading in the Zone will do you a world of good. Trends in forex are determined by  market sentiments based on economic factors. When the fundamentals are sounding good, risk appetite increases the market is in a bullish tone and tend to buy Aud, Nzd, Gbp,Cad and Euro in that order while selling the usd and yen. On the other hand bad economic news induces risk aversion and there will be a stong sells of Aud,Nzd,Gbp,Cad and Euro while buying Usd, Yen. So by looking at the pairings of the risk apetite currencies to the risk aversion( safe haven) currencies on your chart you will immediately know where the market is and if you are using the EA know what side to drive the EA.

In summary risk appetite or risk aversion  sentiments determine the trends in the forex market. You do not need to stay glued to any news service or so called economic analyst, your charts will tell you what sentiments rule the market. For instance the meduim term trend  is bullish the dollar is being sold off and the yen will soon start giving back its gains. For those trading GU with the EA, pls use a 300 pips stop loss for current market conditions, cable is presently too volatile the safe play is eur usd. Samurai thank you for this wonderful thread.

Hi,

Place the EA in say 4H chart, then set Chart_Time_Frame: to 5M - this will monitor the 5M time frame to enter trades,  The trend lines for reducing /closing the SL can them be drawn on the 4H chart.  5M chart need not appear on your screen, although I have it up permanently.

Bye.

--- 帖子 #1544 ---
Hi, here the version 1.5a, i have skip the vs 1.5, was not working correctly.

This version enable you to setup your EA with both long and short.  The way you control the EA side is by identifying the main trend in the trendline description. With this version no need to check your EA side.

"Main_UpTrend_Alert_"  This description will be equivalent to Only Long.  "Main_DownTrend_Alert_" will be equivalent to Only Short.

You can have all the other trendlines descriptions from the other versions, But make sure you have only one trendline with "Main_" in the description. It will still work if  you have more than one with "Main_" in your description, it will take the last one draw with "Main_" in it. But it is not a good habit since it confuse the situation.

This version will also clean your chart from old trendlines that produce erratic results.  Parameter "Trend_line_Keep" control the number of trendline that you want on the chart.

This version will not check for excessive lost on real account.  This was not very reliable so i removed it.

Hope this is not too complex to setup.  Once you are used to that way to describe your trendline, you will not go back to the previous version.  It is also more stable and have a better status description on the left corner.

Best of luck to all.

ActionPl

--- 帖子 #1581 ---
Hi okehiedon,  I also kept getting the "excessive loss" alert and could not figure out why.  So I went into the code and turned it off.

Here is how I did it.

1. open the EA in the editor.  (Right click on the EA name and select Modify)

2. when the editor opens, select EDIT then select FIND

3  in the FIND WHAT box type in "Excessive" then click on the FIND NEXT button.

4.  It will then highlight the line with "excessive" in it.  (See the attached Picture)

5.  Add the  /* and the */ to the line as shown in the attached pictures

6. then press the F5 button to run the compiler.

Done...

Cheers,  DojiMojo

--- 帖子 #1598 ---
This manual will be very useful once it completed.

Here are some comments. Note, that I still learn the system so I may be wrong. I hope Actionpl will come and takes the time to review the manual.

1. The v63H04 (in the name of the expert) is the version number of the original EA which served as a base for the manual driven version.

2. If an integer number is added at the end of the description of the trendline (e.g. "Main_DownTrend_Alert_20") then the trading will be stopped if the price closes the trendline with 20 pips or less. The trading will also be stopped if there is a gap (e.g. on the weekend) and the price emerges on the other side of the trendline.

3. EmailAlert will send Email notification if the trendline is broken or - if the number is set - the price closes the trendline by ZZ pips (e.g. "Main_DownTrend_Alert_ZZ" where ZZ is an integer number).

4. PopupAlert will display a popup alert in MT4 if the trendline is broken or price closes to the trendline as described above.

5. Trend_line_Keep: the EA cleans your chart from old trendlines that produce erratic results. This parameter controls the number of trendline that you want on the chart.

6. Manage_Trade: if true, then the EA will disable the trade if the Heiken Ashii indicator goes against our driving direction.

7. (from the v1.4 version, the quotes are from Actionpl)

'If you put the following description in your trend line: DownTrend_Close_Alert_

As soon the price action will go above the trend line, it will close all sell open trade if it is a DownTrend. If you put as description UpTrend_Close_Alert_ all buy open trade will be close.

This will version will also included the trade hedging function as described in previous post.

If the description is: DownTrend_Trade_Alert_20 it will initiate a buy trade when the price action will be 20 pips above your trend line. As soon the price action will go above your trend line, it reduce the stoploss by the factor that you have given in the "Reduce_factor" variable. Same functionality for the UpTrend but with a sell trade.'

'A trend line with the following word "Close_" will act as described in my previous post. And a trend line with "Trade_" in it will intiate a hedge trade when the trend line is hit.

Note: If the Trendline with a Close in it is hit, the EA will stop trading waiting for your intervention. Any other trendline that is hit will toogle the EA state between able to trade and unable to trade.'

8. TrendLineWatch: (quote from Actionpl) 'If you set variable TrendLineWatch to true, the system will not trade up to a point where the price action hit a trend with an Alert set to it. So if the pair does not trend, you can set two trends on up and one down with Alert to it. When one of those will be hit the system will start to trade the way you have selected.'

9. More parameters are described in the source of the EA. To see them, open the Firebird-v63H04_H_Ashi_Trend_vs1_5b.mq4 with Notepad.

--- 帖子 #1617 ---
Hi see my comment in blue.

1. The v63H04 (in the name of the expert) is the version number of the original EA which served as a base for the manual driven version. ok

2. If an integer number is added at the end of the description of the trendline (e.g. "Main_DownTrend_Alert_20") then the trading will be stopped if the price closes the trendline with 20 pips or less. The trading will also be stopped if there is a gap (e.g. on the weekend) and the price emerges on the other side of the trendline. The interger will have an effect only with the following description "Alert_20" or a trendline with Trade_ in it.  See the updated word file that i just published.

3. EmailAlert will send Email notification if the trendline is broken or - if the number is set - the price closes the trendline by ZZ pips (e.g. "Main_DownTrend_Alert_ZZ" where ZZ is an integer number). Only if trendline is broken. See new word file

4. PopupAlert will display a popup alert in MT4 if the trendline is broken or price closes to the trendline as described above.

5. Trend_line_Keep: the EA cleans your chart from old trendlines that produce erratic results. This parameter controls the number of trendline that you want on the chart.

6. Manage_Trade: if true, then the EA will disable the trade if the Heiken Ashii indicator goes against our driving direction.

7. (from the v1.4 version, the quotes are from Actionpl)

'If you put the following description in your trend line: DownTrend_Close_Alert_

As soon the price action will go above the trend line, it will close all sell open trade if it is a DownTrend. If you put as description UpTrend_Close_Alert_ all buy open trade will be close.

This will version will also included the trade hedging function as described in previous post.

If the description is: DownTrend_Trade_Alert_20 it will initiate a buy trade when the price action will be 20 pips above your trend line. As soon the price action will go above your trend line, it reduce the stoploss by the factor that you have given in the "Reduce_factor" variable. Same functionality for the UpTrend but with a sell trade.'

'A trend line with the following word "Close_" will act as described in my previous post. And a trend line with "Trade_" in it will intiate a hedge trade when the trend line is hit.

Note: If the Trendline with a Close in it is hit, the EA will stop trading waiting for your intervention. Any other trendline that is hit will toogle the EA state between able to trade and unable to trade.'

8. TrendLineWatch: (quote from Actionpl) 'If you set variable TrendLineWatch to true, the system will not trade up to a point where the price action hit a trend with an Alert set to it. So if the pair does not trend, you can set two trends on up and one down with Alert to it. When one of those will be hit the system will start to trade the way you have selected.'

9. More parameters are described in the source of the EA. To see them, open the Firebird-v63H04_H_Ashi_Trend_vs1_5b.mq4 with Notepad.[/quote]

--- 帖子 #1626 ---
HI, Normally if you see waiting for main trend, it mean that the EA does not recognize your Main trend description.  Verify the spelling. If everything is ok, re-initialize the EA by using Key F7 and enter. When you switch time frame, you re-initialize the EA, i think it's why the EA start when you switch to a daily timeframe.

Question#2. You can have as many trendline draw on the chart as you want.  Only the trendline with Main in the description will drive your EA long or short.  All the others will react to your description.  Remember, The EA will switch between normal trade to broken state and back to normal trade each time price action will hit a trendline with an Alert_ in the description.

Switching time frames will not cause the EA to go wrong.  It has his own timeframe control.  Switching time frame on your chart is only what you see, the EA is not using the time frame that you see to take action.  It use what you have set on the variable "Chart_Time_Frame"

Hope this does not confuse you more.  Try it on the simulator to see how it work.

Bye.

--- 帖子 #1633 ---
Hi

Looking at your chart top left corner, it displays "Waiting for Main Trend", this means it does not recognize your trend line. Coding or spelling in your trend-line object is wrong. Double click on your trend-line, then right click on it, select "trend-line properties" option, then "common" - "description" and enter the description as "Main_UpTrend_Alert_". Then, if the EA sees your trendline, it will display in top left, the description "== trades enabled == safe to trade ==".

--- 帖子 #1653 ---
"does the "TS" change the "Stop Loss" in coordination with "Take Profit" and "TS trigger" ONLY as described in "FB EA Settings" YES, it does so only at the beginning of every 5 min if your "Chart_Time_Frame" variable is set at 5.

You can see when the TS is turn on, the following way.  When the TS is trig in accordance to your TS trigger, your trade will not have a T/P (Take profit) number under this col.

ActionPl

Hi crt4x,

Try placing the "Main_UpTrend_Alert_" below the current price action or

"Main_DownTrend_Alert_" above the PA. If the "Main_DownTend_Alert_" line is below current price, the EA sees the trendline as being broken by the price. Trading stops and the "Alert_" is dropped from the trendline description. Hope this works.

--- 帖子 #1692 ---
[quote=Slider;2828215] Hi guys, the rules is has follow.
Assuming that you have set trailingstop at true:

Initially, trail stop is not active.

It will activate itself if PA make your profit bigger than value of TakeProfit minus value of TStrigger.  The order will be modified if at the beginning of the next period of 5 min, your profit is still above your thresshold plus the slip value that you have setup.  In any case the EA will monitor PA and if it fall below your TS, it will close the trade.

You can see from your journal what happen.  If you see Close, it mean that the price action had fall back below the TS excluding the slip value .  If you see modify order, it mean that the EA was able to modify your order because you had enough profit to do it.

Try it with the simulator with number of trade set at 1, you will see how it work.  If you put number of trade greater than 1, it is not obvious to understand since i need to find a way to track many Trailing stop order live.  For now it is working in most situation, but on some occasion the second and subsequent orders follows the max value setup by the first order.  I will look to improve it so it can monitor each trade individually.

Next version later this summer.

Best of luck.

Bye

The fact is, this EA is a top-performing EA, especially with so much work put into it by Actionpl and Samurai Power and I give them all the credit for it. I personally believe the best way to run this EA is to drive it manually if you know how to determine the direction of the Trend fast and accurately, actually, that is what i'm testing with the latest version (manual driving) and it's yielding good result.

The only 2 reasons i'm testing the fully-auto and posting the result are;
1) I'm not really a smaller TF trader - so I checked the bigger TF with the EA - i believe that could reduce the excessive drawdowns - if i'm monitoring the H4 and Daily TFs to determine my trend why can't I trade on it.

2) I believe that if the result continues to be good and consistent, somebody like Actionpl and other talented programmers on this thread will take it from there and perfect it for higher TF traders like me.

I actually don't know if running the EA fully auto will be good long term, but I know its been giving very good result for the past 3 weeks and very low draw down. I tried back-testing the last 2 weeks on a simulator but the result wasn't as good as the actual result i got on live trading (forward testing), so, i'm not going to completely rely on the result of a strategy tester, the best way to find out is to forward test it for sometime and compare it with your backtest result for that period. Also, very important, I don't actually run the EA continously like that, I close all left-over trades before the London market opens on Sunday, i don't care if they are lost trades (as long as I'm in profit already), and I don't activate the EA until the London market opens on Monday morning (2AM EST). I guess that might answer your question - TheGabriel.

PS: I'm trading both the semi-auto and fully-auto on my live accounts now. it's been good. I'm not recommending anyone to do this until you've tested it and satisfied with the result.

Ayo.

--- 帖子 #1724 ---
Those message on left top corner are only there to give us some indcation of what is happening with the EA.

Trade eanable: EA is ready to analyse the market since condition are met

trade disable:: It meant that the EA will not trade due to filter parameters

MarketAnalysis: The EA is checking the trend (if flag is on)

Enterposition: The EA is analysing the actual situation to enter a trade.  Most of time it will not open a new position. If all the conditions are met, it will open a trade.

Best regards

Actionpl

--- 帖子 #1743 ---
Thanks ActionPL for your help.

I have concerns about the risk of this system.

It has a large SL @ 300 pips and opens 5 positions when the market is going against us. Then it hedges those positions. If we are trading 8 pairs the worst case scenario is we have a total of 40 positions open. If the market moves against us (trend change) we could conceivably be in very large drawdown and even margin call. The question then has to be asked, what is our total overall risk to our account (VaR)? I don't think this issue has been adequately addressed? Since we are going down the automated route, perhaps a coder could implement an advanced money management routine to allow the trader to control risk more effectively. I for one think this is a great system but we need to prepare for the worst should it occur.

Any thoughts?

Cheers

Spy

--- 帖子 #1744 ---
Hi,

I'll do these things to control the risk:

1. position size properly to have lotsize number such that 300pips stop is only 1R risk (my 1R is 3% of my total capital)

2. set MaxOpenOrders to 2-3, i see this still yield good result in my backtest

3. use Main_*Trend_Alert_ rather than *_Trade_Alert_ which will not open reverse position when trendline broken

4. use default Reduce_factor=2, it'll cut the stoploss by half when trendline broken. thus, if you have 2 open orders and the trend reverse, the total risk will be lower down to 1R rather than 2R originally

--- 帖子 #1750 ---
The EA will stop openning new trades and will use the Stop lost to close your trade if hit.

You need to switch to version 1.4a if you want the EA to close trades when price action hit your trend line.  To activate this automatic close fonction, you need to insert Close_ in the description.  Ex. UpTrend_Close_Alert_

Bye

--- 帖子 #1751 ---
The new rules will prevent us to have two open positions buy and sell at the end of the day.  So, you can't use the Option Trade_ in your description. (For version 1.4a and up)

The FIFO rule will in fact restrict us to have only one trade open at a given time.  So we will need to set variable MaxOpenOrder = 1.

I did not see any reference that will prevent us to use Stop Lost or Take Profit.

If you have some information about that, please send me the link.

We will need to find a new setup that will produce good results with those constraints.

Bye

ActionPl

--- 帖子 #1780 ---
i found these in the doc in this thread "Instructions for Setting Up and Operating Firebird - June 1 2009.doc"

so if i want to have the EA start trading long on a break of a horizontal trendline (resistance) when in a range i would use #???

i tried various combinations below in strategy tester but, i ended up with buys and sells opening in the test when i only wanted long. i had trendline_watch=true. should trendanalysis be on too by the way for a scenario where i only wanted to initiate trading on the break of a trendline? i tried first with it on and it wouldn't open any trades in this scenario so i turned it off and it started trading but, i got some sell trades when i didn't want any.

i'm using v 1.5c

it would be helpful if there was a quality document created and maintained that covered the evolving trendline syntax and trade examples. i have seen A LOT of people having to ask these specific questions.

thanks for all the generosity in sharing.

1. Alert_30: If price action come close to this trend by 30 pips by either side.
2. DownTrend_Alert_ :If price action come above this trendline
3. UpTrend_Alert_: If price action come below this trendline
4. UpTrend_Close_Alert_: Same as 3 but will close all open buy order
5. DownTrend_Close_Alert_: Same as 2 but will close all open sell order
6. UpTrend_Trade_Alert_30: Same as 3 but will initiate a sell trade if price action go 30 pips below the uptrend
7. DownTrend_Trade_Alert_30: Same as 2 but will initiate a buy trade if price action go 30 pips above the downtrend.
8. UpTrend_Close_Trade_Alert_30: Will close all buy trade before doing 6
9. DownTrend_Trade_Alert_30: Will close all sell trade before doing 7

--- 帖子 #1787 ---
I did some more research on this new rules.  Here the link to read the new rules.  Go at the end of this report.  http://forex-systems-reviews.com/NFAreport.pdf.  This report will also gave you a list of brokers with their responce to those new rules. A MUST TO READ

As you can see, Stoploss and Take profit will still work.

Edging will not work from day to day but will work on a given day.

FIFO rule will prevent us to have multiple order with the same lot size.  So this mean that with version 1.5c and earlier, you will need to set variable

MaxOpenOrders=1 if you want to follow this rule.

There is a way to get around that, it is to have lot size change for eah trade.  I will have to change the EA so it will change the lot size by an increment that you will specify each time a trade is open.  This way, we will not go agains the FIFO rules starting the 1 of August.  So the first trade will be at 0.1 lot, the second trade will be at 0.11 lot and so on.(If the increment is 0.01 and if your broker accept microlot).   I will have the EA customize in such a way that people will be able to select the initial lot size as we have now and the increment.  So you will be able to customize it to your broker requirement.

I can't guarantee that this will be ready for the 1st of August since it required change to the code and i will be in vacation.   So next version will have this feature and the improvement on trailling stop fonction as described last week.

Have a great summer.

Bye

Actionpl

--- 帖子 #1788 ---
I think to have a better risk managemend we should include in the EA code, the strategy of scaling in and out of positions, basically let's say we have this situation:

1) We open a trade of 0,3 lots with tp of 90 pips.
2) At +30 pips the robots closes 0,1 of the position and moves the take profit to breakeven.
3) At +60 pips the robots closes the other 0,1 of the position and if the price goes to +90 pips we're out with a total of 180 pips with 0,1 lotsize, if not it will go to the stoploss wich is at breakeven and we don't lose a penny and we get 90 pips with 0,1 lot size.

If you don't get it, see here

There already are some ea that do this but we can attach 2 eas on the same chart so we have to include it in the code or have 2 MT4 opened for the same account with the 2 eas attached.

This is my first post on FX factory, mostly because I didnt feel I had enough forex knowlege until now to make an edjucated post.

Anyways here it goes... I have been up and down this thread expermenting with different settings for the multiple Firebird EA's that are available. I have been using a strategy utilizing these systems on a live account for about a month now and has shown to be profitable. I know a month is short term however I have a good reason to believe the strategy will work for long term as well.

The strategy utilizes both full auto and semi driven firebirds.

As TheGabriel has mentioned the full auto system works very well on a ranging market but not trending.

So I have been trading 8 currencies at a time (the number of charts works well in a verticle sortment on MT4) and placing the fully auto firebird on only markets that are ranging, and then placing the semi auto firebird on the markets that are trending.

My results have been very pleasing. I have about 85% win rate and all my losses occured with the trending market which I have the semi auto version running which reduces S/L to 150 pips. Also my gains in the trending markets have been higher due to trailing S/L.

Now, I understand that the system can draw down your account and cause margin call, however if that happens it is most likely due to poor money management. Such as the above post having $900 and working with .1 (mini) lots. With that high of a risk he only needed 3 losses on the full auto ea and his account is vanished! 3 losses!!! IMO that is not good money management. I have been trading micro .01 lots and will increase the lot size by .01 every $200-$300 made. This way before I even reach the mini lot size I will have close to $5,000 in the account.

I am not an experienced trader (only about 3 months experience) but I do know good money management and I do know a good system when i see one and i believe this is it, I just hope it works long term.

Thats just my .02 cents

--- 帖子 #1828 ---
Hi ayoneeyee and others, try this version, it has many new features and some bugs fix.

New features:

1- Will change the trade size by what is in variable "Lots_Increment" each time a new trade is activated while having a trade open. This will allow us to go around the FIFO rule.
2- Allow to have hidden profit and hidden stoploss when variable "TrailingStopFlag" is true.  Lood at variable "Hidden_Take_Profit". To desactivate Hidden profit, set this variable larger than the TakeProfit variable. To activate the hidden stop lost, you need to have profit larger than "TakeProfit-TStrigger".  So if your TakeProfit is at 1000, set your TStrigger at 1010. This way your hidden stoplost will be what you have set in variable TrailingStop as soon the trade is open.

3- A new dynamic trailingStop feature have been added. If you want your trailing stop to be the previous low from time frame set by variable "Auto_Chart_time" which is lower than the (acual Bid - TrailingStop_margin) for a buy, set variable TrailingStopDynamic at true

4- Now the EA will take track of individual trailingStop for a given pair even if you have many trade open on the same pair.

5- Fix bugs in trailingStop fonction

6- For those who are using the TrendLine_watch = true, The EA will automatically place a Main_XTrend_Alert_ when price action will touch either an UpTrend_Alert_ or a DownTrend_Alert_.  So on a flat market, you can place a UpTrend_Alert_ under the lows and a DownTrend_Alert_ above the trading range and when price action will hit the UpTrend_Alert_ trend line, it will trace a Main_Down_Alert_ above the last high of the time frame set by variable "Auto_Chart_time". And the opposite if it hit the DownTrend. Whith this fonction you can set your EA to monitor the market and start trade when conditions are met.

Try this version and let me know how it work.  Make sure your trade on demo with this version before you go live.  This have many tool in the tool boxe to set up your trades. So you need to experiment and get confident with it before doing any life trade.

Best regards

Actionpl

--- 帖子 #1838 ---
So if we consider the market flat, you suggest in Autotrade Section to set Manage_Trade = true and in TrendAnalysis Section to set TrendLine_Watch = true and TrendAnalysis = false.
Manage_Trade is only a flag to prevent the EA to trade agains Heiken Ashi indicator. This indicator is working well with trend. On trendless period, you are going to get hit with badtrade.
TrendLine_Watch flag is to set the EA in a mode to detect when to start trade. So in trendless period, you set this flag at true and place an UpTrend_Alert and a DownTrend_Alert so when price action hit one of those, it will start to trade in the direction that the market want to go. So your skill of how to place those trendline are very important.
So if you combine both of those flag and your are right to detect a trend, it will produce good results.

Bye
Actionpl

Version 3.1a nerver existed. It was a typing mistake. When you see 3.1a it meant 1.3a. I do not recommend to use those old version. They have bug in it. Use version 1.5d.

ActionPl

--- 帖子 #1854 ---
Hi Inquisitor, version 1.5d have a variable that allow to have profit taken which is hidden from broker.  Check this variable "Hidden_TakeProfit" in section Trailing Stop.  P.S.  you need to activate trailing stop in order to have this feature to take effect.

Also the default setup have trailing stop activated and the dynamic trailing stop activated.  This feature will change the trailling stop to the previous bar low or high. This is a good feature for pair with high volatility.  If you don't want that feature, set variable "TrailingStopDynamic" to false.

P.S.  I will have to release a new version to fix a small bug with functionnality of Hidden profit in case of sell order.  Hidden profit does not work for sell order in vesrsion 1.5d. I forgot a line of code....

Bye

Actionpl

--- 帖子 #1857 ---
Hi everyone,

For those interested in using this EA as fully automatic, when the Vs1_5c is not suitable.

Using this live. I have not made big profits, I'm happy if I get 20-25 pips/day - I think the secret is in defining when straight-lining /ranging starts and ends.  I keep getting it wrong!

Use Vs 1_3b only when "straight-lining", and set to trade both "long & short" - NOT during trends, which will clean you out. Therefore, you need to also "drive" 3b but in a different way compared to 5c and 5d where you use trend-lines. I use it on a 5 min chart. Only use when trends dissappear - check the PA - put MA 10, MA 21, MA 50 on your chart, and when they criss-cross often then switch the EA ON.  Soon as they split-up and start moving out of the trade price range area that you assess as suitable for trading the EA, then you switch the EA OFF. Once OFF, I trade manually - when conditions right, the Philip Nel 5M Intra-day System with the above MA 10, 21 and 50 - see his thread http://www.forexfactory.com/showthread.php?t=11854.  When a major trend continues for more than a day, I look to using vs1_5c.

Once 3b is set and running, I check on it periodically (every 1 hr)  to see developing trends and perhaps switch-off.  When I switch-off, I kill the last trade if PA is going wrong way.  Do not trade it within 1 - 2 hours before major news items - switch off.

Saw an earlier post where large SL is used with 3b.  Not a good idea, it WILL clean you out.  The nature of 3b is such that if you run it with TP40 and SL40 for +4 weeks, then it will be like flipping a coin, will come out about square, but with some big draw-downs.  Overall, a 80TP and 40SL will give better returns, but the draw-downs can get VERY big. In back-testing, over  broken 6 week ranging periods, net profits were +570 pips - it did have 6-8 consecutive loss trades in one period.  This is all to stressful.

I prefer using a small TP of 5, max 8. SL 100 is for emergency only, I kill the last trade when I detect a trend starting. I use pairs with small spread - EU, UJ.   Multi pairs can be profitable, but when trends develope, it can become frantic to reduce potential losses.

FB Vs1_3b Settings used are (4 digit broker):

Chart_Time_Frame = 5

MA_Length           = 10

MA_Timeframe       = 15

MAtype                = 0

Percent                = 0.05

TradeonFriday        = 1

Slip                      = 10

Lots                     = 0.nn

MaxOpenOrders      = 1 (keep it simple)

SafeArea               = 5000

PipStep                 = 25 (try smaller numbers, yes?)

TakeProfit              = 5

StopLoss               = 100 (try 40 or 60, yes?)

TrailingStopFlag      = false

TrailingStop           = 40

TStrigger               = 20

MinMarginLevel       = 25.0

Trade from / to       = your preference, I only switch on when I'm available to "supervise" the EA

DivergenceLimit       = 0.005 (0.10 for Jpy pairs)

Other fields - use defaults

Enjoy your trading!

Andy

Hi, the only think i can see that can cause this kind of behavior is the following.

When you have trace a new Main trendline, you must have put it to close from the Price Action. When you trace a trend line close to price action, do it fast and don't put it too close of PA.

Hi markpips,

I had the same problem, so I'm trying the following to correct the situation:

I generally use the Demark trend (daily) for entry. I use default settings except for the usdjpy or eurjpy DivergenceLimit which needs to be increased (default is .002). I didn't know what to use, so I kept increasing until the error disappeared. I settled on .01. After entry I move the trend line down/up to about the SL and this gives the PA room for retracements. I also use the Sonic Channel to confirm the trend. I am comfortable with a 2 to 3 o'clock up channel angle for a buy or 4 to 5 o'clock down channel angle for a sell. Same for the trend lines. Also I try not to enter a buy near the top of a channel or a sell near the bottom of a channel. Don't forget to use money management to determine your lot size. I risk 1 to 1.5 percent so that my loss isn't too great when a trade goes the wrong way. Once a trailing stop is established, I just let it go. Good luck.

--- 帖子 #1877 ---
Hi alain1,

After establishing your trend line, double click on it so that the three boxes appear on you trend line. Next right click on the trend line and select trendline properties on the drop down. Write Main_UpTrend_Alert_, etc. on the description line. Be careful to pay atention to the caps. In order to view what you wrote you have to select any blank area of the chart and right click. Select properties on the dropdown. Select the Common Tab and check the bottom box "Show object descriptions". Trendline inscriptions should now appear. Discussions about this start on page 107 or 108. I'm having problems with 1.5d so I'm still using 1.5c. Good luck.
