--- 帖子 #1883 ---
Hello Fellow Traders,

I have just finished reading a few dozen posts in this thread. It seems very similar to an idea I had a year or so ago. Not having read the entire thread it might have already been discussed but here goes. Having written a few automatic trading systems myself the key to any good system of course is filtering out the little bumps in the road so as not to place a trade too early. Even a trend line won't do that. It can really irritate the trader watching the PA continuing on its merry way after you already jumped off the train.

Now I'm most likely posting this way too early in my understanding of this method but what caught my attention was the mentioning of a trend line. If you are manually drawing or even a code drawn line the buy and sell signals are still the same. Even with trend lines a bump in the road will occur and filtering these is critical to maximizing the trades.

I have experimented with many different methods and one that seems to work the best is the stochastic K & D values. The mistake most coders of EA's do is write values to cross a fixed position or values such as the K value crossing a value of 80 signals a buy which is totally wrong as even the value 100 shows up in the middle of a long uptrend. The other problem is the PA reaching a high pivot point and never hitting 80 which makes the trade a loser when the PA promptly falls off a cliff.

The best way to move the trade forward after hitting a high mark such as a trend line cross over or an indicator cross of a value is to have a filter such as stochastics K less than D on sells or D less than K on longs with adjustable settings. Let’s look at some examples below:

On the M5 chart the PA moves across a trend line after a long down trend which ended at 9:00. The filter checks the value of stochastics K vs. D only after the first requirement of crossing the trend line is met.

K Long setting = 5, K Short setting = 5

EXAMPLE “A”

9:00 PA = 1.5000 K = 5, D = 8

9:05 PA = 1.5010 K = 20, D = 12, Long trade is made.

EXAMPLE “B”

9:00 PA = 1.5000 K = 5, D = 8

9:05 PA = 1.5010 K = 13, D = 12, Long trade is NOT made.

9:10 PA = 1.5020 K = 25, D = 18, Long trade is made.

The PA can actually reverse and the initial trade never made due to the K settings not being reached. A second trade takes over at a much lower PA level which is what we are trying to accomplish.

Other things must also be coded into the EA such as severe downtrends where a counter trend trade is particularly foolish and doesn’t move enough to cover the cost. This can be accomplished with simple codes and why most programs do not address this is crazy. At the very least counter trend trades should be looked at as topping out after crossing a MA-9 value and the K & D filter initiated after reaching no matter what the K or D value or what the slope of the PA for that matter. This will lock in positive trades before reversing in the middle of Bollinger Band channels. You will notice a lot of times the Stochastics value has reached a maximum value although the PA has topped out in the middle of an LRC, Price Channel or Bollinger Band Channel. Another way to recognize the PA trend is the Upper and Lower Bollinger Band values which keeps the trade from ever happening in a quickly consolidating PA. If you can stay out of the bad part of town you will stay a lot healthier.

On an EA which includes stochastics I’ve had success with settings such as 5 and 95 on the K low and high settings which are the high success trades. After back testing the high success trades I then code the harder trades such as countertrend trades.

I’ve also used this method with great success by adding code for Doji recognition and then initiating the filter. Any high or low value of any indicator seems to work great. The program just ignores all other bumps in the road unless a setting is hit to initiate the filter and thus a buy or sell signal. An exception is when the PA is in tight consolidation and trades are halted. If a trade is already in progress then it plays out. Drawing a channel of the consolidation with the PA highs and lows and initiating the filter after a break up or down restarts the program.

Another useful add-in is code for the sudden huge moves that can move the stochastic K value from zero to 100 in one bar and then back down again the next bar. Percent of PA increase and decrease can handle these moves and buy or sell before initiating the filter. The possible downside is if the PA continues moving in that direction such as with some of the violent reversal moves at the start of this recession. Once all of your indicators top out and the PA is still moving though the roof, now what do you do? This actually happened to me as I was watching the EA trade the PA crossed an Upper Bols Band and stochastics K value hit 100. I was sitting with a nice profit and was waiting for the Short trade when the PA shot up like a rocket on the next bar and then the next and the next. A $6,000 additional move just occurred and I’m still in the game. The sell trade was finally satisfied. I had just redone the code from a hard sell at 100 to using the filter. I was just lucky this didn’t happen after a down bar and then it wood have hit my sell stop which is a large $400 per contract. Having anything less then that means you don’t trust your own program to handle the bumps in the road.

The other thing that keeps showing up is all the excuses being made why their EA didn’t work at a particular time or doesn’t work on some currency pairs. That to me is just plain bull crap. A chart is a chart whether its currency pairs, stocks or whatever. Either the program works or it doesn’t work. It’s just that simple. I just read one that starts out saying his program was designed for GBPUSD. I’d like to know how he did that. What he should have said was it was the only pair that made any money and on all the rest he lost his butt. He’s publishing this hoping someone with more intelligence and trading experience can fix his screw-ups.

All of the above I learned the hard way and I’m hoping some of you young coders will learn something about programming an EA from this. One thing I must add is the RSI indicator I would stay clear of as a filter as it doesn’t work well in this type of set-up. Another is the simple fact that unless the EA is based on a trend line with an indicator for filtering the cross all single indicator EA’s are not going to work all of the time or will they work on all charts. The fact is they will blow up your account.

I have back tested this on the Daily chart with a semi-auto system over a 1 1/2 year period with only one loss of $50. I also did a similar test on the one hour with vitually the same results but just more trades. It works on all charts and on all time frames. I just don't have it for MT4 which is why I'm looking here at thia system.

I hope this helps somebody and also hoping somebody that is a great coder takes the bull by the horns and programs these ideas into this program.

Trade well and prosper,

Johnny

Hello Prakash,

Sorry I took so long to answer back. The point I was as making was the 5-8 EMA cross is garbage. The K-D values are much better but there are a number of better signals. Understand the optimum K-D values will vary with the settings of the stochastics.

The other key point is the program itself which is not a bad visual aid for guiding the trader over a few bumps in the road but fails to stop the train at the main terminal so you can get off with maximum pips. The train by passes the station by five miles. The getting on the train is just as dangerous as by the time it finds out the direction it's heading a lot of it's cargo of pips got run over by the train.

The solution and the way to design and code an efficient EA is to jump to the high/low points on the higher time frames. After the PA has reached these high/low points based on user input such as 80-20 stochastic values the trade is moved to the M1 chart values. The code then loops the exit/entry criteria such as the K-D values or a trailing stop is initiated. Both actually are necessary depending on the S & R values reached which again are user input values.

The S & R values are indicators such as the Bollinger Bands or other lines of S & R. This method ignores all of the bumps in the road and it goes from point A to Z ignoring B-Y.

It really is the most logical way to get to Z. If you were planning a trip from NY to LA the quickest and most direct route is to take a jet. This way the Mississippi River and the Rocky Mountains are not bumps in the road we have to worry about. Now the fact is that sometimes the jet might land in Reno and you have to board another flight but you will get to LA in the end.

This type of trading system tells you the plane first has to go by way of Boston and leaves three hours late. It then lands in Chicago and lets you off without a continuing flight and no refund. When you finally get a flight out to LA at additional expense it by passes LA by 500 miles. They give you a parachute so you can jump out and hopefully land on a small deserted island in the middle of the Pacific Ocean. You're very reluctant to do this but the Plane is out of gas and going to crash land anyway so you jump. Now your praying and hoping you land safely but the cold hard fact is the water is shark infested and the landing zone is very small. Don't forget to close your eyes if you're like me and afraid of the sight of your own blood. LOL.

The sharks (Professional traders) are always looking for juicy little snacks like you as we never stop eating.

So if you're going to write an EA you must design it around good S & R values as well as a decent Entry and Exit. Without thoroughly understanding how to trade, no EA will fix that problem. The coder will only code to his ability and knowledge of trading or the lack of it which is so prevalent on the internet.:nerd:

I see posts on many forums proclaiming money making EA's only to find a close to 50-50 win/lose ratio and bigger losses then winners. This one proudly shows a $12 million plus loss and a $9 million win and proclaims a 1.7 profit factor. Now I'm not an Einstein when it comes to math but even Jethro of the Beverly Hillbillies with a sixth grade education could figure this is not a good system.

I had a retired engineer call me on the phone after posting on an automatic trading system thread asking me for advice about a system he was purchasing to supplement his retirement income. He stated it was a real money maker and it only cost $1400 initially and $400 a month there after. I asked him to email the analysis so I could see the win loss ratio and the $ loss / $ investment ratio on both the back and forward tests. He said he didn't have any of that type of information but the program produced 53% wins. I could tell by the way this guy was talking that his mind was already made up and no explanation of the facts from me was going to change this pilgrim's direction to the promise land. Now if an Engineer can be so stupid and not recognize that just flipping a coin will get you 50% then what is the hope of the multitude of people that can't grasp basic math and believe everything they read like the Martian found walking around NY or the talking pig in Iowa. I think our government hires way too many of these people and makes them bank examiners. They're all members of the "Be Kind to Dumb Animals Club". I think it's their natural preservation instinct.

Let me know how you make out with this EA.

Happy trades,

Johnny

Undoubtedly you're a newbie or at the very least not versed in the qualities of a good EA. Don't be blinded by the profits shown on the website as a better gauge of the good, the bad and the ugly is the losses and the profit factor. The profit factor of 1.9 is very low to the point of ridiculas. Anybody worth their salt as a trader could write a better performimg EA blind folded. My very first attempt at writing an EA as a newbie coder many years ago was 50 times higher than this.

Understand that a professional trader looks for no less then 95% wins and would expect no less from an EA. This EA isn't even in the same ballpark and is obviously written by somebody who doesn't fully understand trading. The problem with these incomplete EA's is they can look good on some currency pairs some of the time but fail miserably most of the time. They cannot be traded on any chart or security and the seller will usually say I wrote this EA around a particular currency pair which is pure bull crap. The truth be known is that they kept looking until they found one that showed a profit. A decent EA will work on any chart whether it be currency, stocks or options. The mathematical formulas behind an EA don't know the difference between stocks or currency pairs because it's all just looking at the numbers.

There are a few fair producing EA's on the internet but this isn't one of them. I've only ever found one worth anything at all. If you invest a dime on something like this you're an idiot and you should have the letters "DFI" tattood on your forehead.

--- 帖子 #1892 ---
I didn't posted in this thread for soooooo looong.

I still belive this EA is one of the best I come cross to.

One of the easiest method for driving this bad boy would probably be with a simple Parabolic SAR indicator. Its critical we found best trending pairs and deal with them. Actually this EA makes also good resolds in sideways market with both Long and Short option on.

So the idea is...pull up daily/weekly chart best trending pairs you could find (e/u g/u..itc). Plot simple Parabolic SAR and drive the EA with the trend flow.

Small swings might hurt us a little as the indicator change direction, but real money is on big swings. Where loses should be covered.

--- 帖子 #1902 ---
This is a script created by Steve Hopwood that sets/adjusts stops, opens/closes trades, steps, trails...basically a complete trade management tool.

I use it quite often to set a global % SL so that of all trades that are open, it can take profit or stop loss at a defined $ amount or %. You can set it to only affect a particular magic number or all trades, etc. There's quite a bit of documentation + the tool ((free) at the site below.

Hope you guys find it as useful as I do,

Cheers,

--- 帖子 #1914 ---
gasgas

Thank you for your question. I trade with the 30/60/120 ema  on the 4hr as part of my trading repertiore that includes the (GU intraday system-my creation). Now the key to using this EA as long as price remains below the 120 ema with the 30 and 60 ema in line, I remain short and vice versa. I only change when I have a daily close above or below the 120 ema. (I adjust the ea only on a daily close.

Then I enter the trade in the direction of the new trend. At this time I am watching the last swing low or high on the 4 hr as a confirmation of the new trend as long as price does not break below that low the new trend is valid(definetly there would be a pull back).

Otherwise the simpler way is to search for pairs with already established trends using the 3 emas and drive the ea that way. For example this is the chart of the euraud, you can see what happened when price broke the 120 ema on the 4 hr price pulled back and found support there. This also concided with the 1.4000 round number barrier zone. So we have a daily close above and I will drive the ea long until price breaks below and closes off the 120 ema on a daily close. Trading like this you would have less whipsaws and catch those big moves that the forex market is known for.

It also gives you time to check up on the market news and know what is driving price action, thereby giving you more confidence on your trades. I hope this helps.

Alright guys sorry, I did not answer your questions immediately.

1. I trade all the majors including the major exotic pairs.

2. I trade the EA with the ATR value of each pair. i trade using 3 trades for each pair with a total risk exposue of 6 per cent

3. I first run through all the pairs looking for established trends using the 30/60/120 ema. These are the pairs I give priority. Then I keep my eyes on potential trades. Go through the charts with just the 3 emas and you can see how effective this system is.

4. I use the same ea on this thread, i just drive the ea either short or long.

5. Never trade without a stop loss.

6. I use the default pip step but may adjust by 10-20 pips depending on the volatility of the pair.

7. Fundamentally, I am always long audusd and audjpy cause of the high interest rate differential.

--- 帖子 #1922 ---
Zukies thanks for the complement, but actually is nothing new.

Please take note we only trade the 4hr chart and not daily. The EMAs are only for the 4 hr chart.

For example when price breaks above the 120 ema on the 4hr chart.We would like to see a daily close with price above the 120 ema on the 4hr chart. Before we have a valid change of trend and thereby drive the EA in that direction.

You would now place the EA main trend line to pass through the swing low of the price swing that broke the 120 ema, because usually price would retrace and if it is a valid change of trend it would not break that low. So we would have the ea enter the new trend at a discount (usually I use 40 pips step on the usd pairs and 50-55 on the jpy pairs). This was the case with the eurusd which I immensely benefited from.

The euraud as I adviced in my earlier post is already in an uptrend , remember break of 120 ema on 4hr chart and if you had entered as I showed in the chart I posted earlier you would already be in the money.

But guys note that I stop driving the ea in the direction of the trend when the daily chart is overdone. That is when the daily rsi is above 70 or under 30. It means a reversal may be in place and usually price at such levels reverse quickly.

I hope this helps

--- 帖子 #1923 ---
greven if you have traded the ea on this thread you would see it has a provison for entering the number of trades you want as price moves against you.

Every Pair has a different daily range value and we want to have realisitc stop loss and take profit levels. For example the daily range of EU is 138. So I calculate my stop loss/ take profit  using values from 1, 1.5 or 2  x ADR. What that means is that we would survive any minor retracement against the trend and enter on a discount as the ea takes trades in the direction of the prevailing trend. Because we have used realistic take profit levels we expect our objective to be hit within 2 days and as price retraces the ea enters at a discount and the cycle continues.

Remeber when you are trend trading you can only be wrong once. That is when the trend breaks and reverses. Off course the EA,s trend line functionality is an added advantage as it reduces the stop loss by half if price touches the trend line.

Also note that  we want to identify and profit from the meduim term trend. That is why we use the 30/60/120 ema on the 4hr. A quick look through all the charts in your charting package would reveal how few whipsaws you would have using the 3EMAs to determine trend direction.

--- 帖子 #1924 ---
Finally before I take my break today.

To help confirm the trend direction when trading USD pairs apply the 30/60/120 ema on a 4 hr chart of the US Dollar Index(professional trading tip). The trend on that index will determine dollar stength or weakness on all your forex pairs.

For yen pairs the general rule is Usd Jpy determines overall trend direction of the yen pairs. However it is not as definite as the dollar index. In most cases when the dollar is weak on all fronts the other yen pairs are quite choppy.

--- 帖子 #1941 ---
I do not use a fixed tp/sl. I usually use 1.5 Atr to set my stops and targets. The rational behind the 1.5 is that in my opinion on a healthy trend price will pull back but would not close below the previous day low. So I believe that if price pulls back and hits my stops which is 1.5 ATR then the trend is weakening.

You could limit your DD by manipulating these 2 variables in the settings:
The settings for back tests are as follows:

s0="Section for Trend Analysis"; TrendAnalysis=false;   EmailAlert=false;  PopupAlert=false;  TrendLine_watch=false;   Reduce_factor=2; Trend_line_Keep=3; AutoTrend_timeperiod=240;   s1="Section for Autotrade"; Manage_Trade=false;   Heiken_Ashi_timeperiod=240; index=1; email=false;  s2="Section for  FireBird"; Chart_Time_Frame=5; MA_length=21;  MA_timeframe=5; MAtype=1;  Percent=0.05; TradeOnFriday=1; slip=25;  Lots=0.1; MaxOpenOrders=5;  SafeArea=10000; PipStep=100; TakeProfit=1000;  Stoploss=2000;  s3="Section for Trailing stop"; TrailingStopFlag=false;   TrailingStop=200; TStrigger=200; MinMarginLevel=250; TradeFrom1=0;   TradeUntil1=24; TradeFrom2=0; TradeUntil2=0; TradeFrom3=0;   TradeUntil3=10; TradeFrom4=0; TradeUntil4=0; s4="Section for   iFXAnalyzer"; Fast_Period=23; Fast_Price=1; Slow_Period=84;   Slow_Price=1; DivergenceLimit=0.1; Use_V63D_Divergence=false;   IncreasementType=0; PipsLoss=500; GMT=2; DST=0; OpeningHour=0;   ClosingHour=24; writelog=0;

MaxOpenOrders=5 (max. no. of open trades at one time floating); reducing this...will surely decrease the drawdown..

PipStep=100 (opens a trade at every 10 pips); increase to 20 or 40, would reduce the DD as well..

But, keep in mind that this will reduce your gains significantly.

But, now..with this grid trader..it doesnt have to satisfy any entry conditions for it to take trades..but just the movement of price up or down in our predefined grid steps or intervals...and it will start doing its job!!

--- 帖子 #1987 ---
The method or concept is the same as the one I explained before..

in my earlier posts..

but..I just changed it to grid trader ea.

Attached please find my screen shots of euro 4h chart with the cornflower tpl.

The way I take trades or start my automation of trades (meaning in real  time : turn on the grid trader ea), is when the price crosses the cornflower  EMA...i.e. EMA 24....

AND at the same time I use this same EMA as my stop loss...

so, my stop loss is being moved along the 24 ema up or down, depending on the direction of the trend..

This is the foundation.

(please understand this is a deviation from the cornflower entry method...

as explained by Lever70

http://www.forexfactory.com/showpost...00&postcount=1)

I am using cornflower 4H only to monitor my trades visually.

attachments titled eurusd 1, and 2

shows where I enter (Yellow line)

and my exit (red line)..

REMEMBER, cornflower EMA is controlling my entry and exit.

(The blue areas in the screen shots are supposed to be  where the  trading hit some losses..as you can see, its minimal number of  pips  provided that the EA is controlled by the 24 ema/cornflower)
